The Wan Case Begins Negotiations 62

First Contact in Changchun

The Two Sides' Views Are Far Apart

Changchun Correspondence - Negotiations on the Wan case will be resolved locally. Our side is represented by Zhong Yu, negotiator for Jilin and Hebei, and the Japanese side is represented by Ishikawa, the Japanese Consul General in Jilin. Both Zhong and Ishikawa returned to Jilin from Liaoning and had a meeting on the 27th at the Changchun Foreign Affairs Office. (1) Our side firmly insisted that stopping construction, withdrawing troops, abolishing the weir, and rescinding the contract were prerequisites before discussing the issue of compensation for the losses of Korean farmers. (2) The Japanese side insisted that our side acknowledge the complete validity of the land rental contract for rice cultivation before discussing the complete withdrawal of Japanese troops and police. They did not comment on our side's demands to stop construction, abolish the weir, and rescind the contract, or on the issue of compensation for Korean farmers. Zhong argued that Ishikawa's insistence on his views was tantamount to going against the spirit of neighborly friendship and sincerely seeking truth and justice. Only when the views were closer could the negotiations be put on track; otherwise, there would be no hope of resolution. Ishikawa believed that what our side had proposed was unreasonable and not a prerequisite. It must be known that our territory had been invaded, and our farmland had been destroyed. The facts are all there, and the current situation can be investigated. No matter which country it is, it is afraid that it will be difficult to endure. Putting oneself in another's position, it is inevitable. Ishikawa had no words to respond to this. Zhong also said that if the Consul General takes the contract as a prerequisite before discussing the withdrawal of Japanese troops, it would be difficult to comply. Regardless of whether the land lease procedures are complete or not, the Changchun County Government only approved the review and verification, and there was no formal approval. During this review period, the lease was not submitted to the county for review. According to the regulations of Jilin regarding Korean people renting rice fields, 1. Only Korean people who have naturalized as Chinese and obtained a citizenship certificate, 2. Must first submit a request for registration, attach the lease, and then send personnel to verify and report, and after approval, issue a formal rice cultivation license to be valid. The Korean farmers did not complete these two procedures, and without waiting for the county government's approval, they forcibly occupied the people's farmland, started construction, built weirs, and dug trenches, which was a clear violation of the legitimate and inherent land rights of Chinese farmers. Moreover, Hao Yongde claimed that he rented the land for self-cultivation, hiring dozens of Korean farmers to guide the work, and did not state that he was subletting to Korean people for rice cultivation. It was purely a fraudulent means to seek the approval of our government. The conspiracy was exposed, and the right to land ownership was harmed. If this case were discovered within Japan, how could it be approved? As for saying that Korean farmers are poor and have a difficult life, giving them special consideration and allowing them to continue to cultivate rice is not only impossible to do because the land belongs to the people, but there is also no reason to allow them to forcibly occupy the land of the landowner. Although this consultation was not a formal negotiation, there were many arguments from both sides. As a result, Ishikawa agreed to telegraph the Japanese government for instructions on our demand to withdraw troops and stop construction and would schedule another consultation after receiving instructions. Zhong Yu will also telegraph the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Northeast Political and Military Council to report the situation of the consultation with Ishikawa and request instructions. Ishikawa telegraphed Tokyo for instructions on that day, and as of the 4th, there is still no reply, and the negotiations have been suspended in name only. (July 28th)

Andong Refugees

The Shelter is Closed Again 63

Refugees Show No Intention of Returning to Korea

An-tung dispatch: The disaster-stricken compatriots who had fled from the Korean border to seek refuge here have been successively provided with funds and dispersed. On the 26th and 27th, suddenly 469 refugees arrived from Pyongyang and Wonsan. They were again taken into the First Shelter for accommodation. The head of the An-tung Public Security Bureau, Zhang Hanwei, considering the large number of refugees and the substantial daily expenses, instructed the refugees to decide where they wished to go and to depart as soon as possible, not to stay in An-tung for long. As a result, 145 refugees boarded the Jitong steamer for Tianjin on the 28th, 45 for Qingdao, and 5 for Dalian. Others sought employment in this port city or went to Heilongjiang Province, with many going to the Tonghua and Linjiang areas. In addition to providing train and ship tickets from the shelter, each person was given a small sum of one silver dollar for expenses. By 3 p.m. on the 29th, the dispersal was completed, and the shelter was closed again. It is said that the expenses within these three days amounted to more than 2,000 yuan. It has been found that most of the 400-plus refugees have gone to other ports to make a living, with none showing any desire to return to Korea. This is because they are mostly laborers, who had spent years building up their homes and possessions in Korea. This unfortunate catastrophe has caused them to lose everything, so they feel deeply saddened and unwilling to return to such a dangerous place. On the 29th, a little after 5 p.m., another 50 refugees arrived from Pyongyang. Twenty-five of them were taken in by relatives and friends, while the remaining 25, being poor and destitute, were sent by the Public Security Bureau to the Mao Xing Inn on Zhongfu Street for temporary lodging, and they will be provided with funds for dispersal within the next few days. At present, the large group of refugees have scattered, with only a dozen or so receiving treatment at the An-tung Shi Hospital due to severe injuries or other illnesses suffered in Korea. The medical expenses are paid entirely from donations, and after they recover, they will be provided with funds for dispersal. According to statistics, all the refugees who have come to An-tung have been received with donations from various sources, totaling over 18,000 yuan, of which approximately 14,000 yuan has been spent. There is currently a remaining donation of over 4,000 yuan. (July 30th)

Unprecedented Flood in Hanshi 64

A Sudden Breach in the Upper Section of Shandongmen

Over Five Hundred People Swept Away

Water Depth in the City Exceeds Twenty Feet

Hankou dispatch: The Shandongmen railway gate, which protects Hanshi, collapsed at 7:50 a.m. on the 2nd due to the excessive water force. Following the breach of the Danshuichi embankment, the entire city was submerged by noon. The prosperous marketplaces were instantly transformed into a flooded land. The losses suffered by the people are incalculable. It is truly an unprecedented disaster. The details are recorded below:

Shandongmen Breached: After the Danshuichi embankment was breached, the waters of Houhu approached the railway. The Shandongmen, located above the Charity Association, and the Shuangdongmen near Jisheng Wumalu became crucial pillars. The government also increased its defenses. Chen Keming, Director of the Water Conservancy Bureau, Fang Dazhi, Director of the Construction Department, He Baohua, Mayor of Hankou, and Wang Shiliu, Director of the Public Security Bureau, and others made regular inspections. Residents of Houhu, whose homes had been turned to ruins, gathered on the roads to assist in the rescue efforts. From the 29th, they guarded day and night without rest. On the evening of the 1st, the water level rose, and the Shandongmen and Shuangdongmen showed signs of imminent collapse. On the morning of the 2nd, the upper section of the Shandongmen suddenly breached, and over 500 refugees on the road were swept away by the raging torrent. The sounds of wailing shook the heavens and the earth.

The Entire City Submerged: After the breach of Shandongmen, the floodwaters rushed in, swift as a whirlwind. From the Charity Association along Jisheng Wumalu, the Municipal Government, Sanxin Street, and other places, the houses were submerged to the rooftops, to a depth of over twenty feet. Zhongshan Road and Xinsheng Road were submerged to a depth of four or five feet. Traffic was immediately cut off, and shops were forced to close. People climbed onto rooftops or took refuge in trees, in a state of utter distress. He Chengjun, the Chief of the Military Affairs Office, Liu Wendao, the Director of Civil Affairs, and Xia Douyin, the Garrison Commander, immediately hired small boats and, together with the Charity Association and other organizations, went to the flooded areas to rescue the victims. Many were rescued and sent to the Fourth Bureau of Wuchang Cotton, Hemp, and Silk for shelter, and the emergency relief committee distributed food rations to alleviate hunger.

Maintaining Order: The Wuhan Garrison Command, due to the excessive floodwaters, and in order to maintain public order, submitted a request to the Military Affairs Office and declared a special curfew from the 29th of last month.

Puduo Mountain Special Announcement: We hereby announce that we have heard that some unlawful monks on our mountain are violating the precepts and intentionally causing trouble, hiding in Shanghai and colluding with unscrupulous merchants to sell all the tall buildings on the mountain to a certain country, hoping to obtain huge sums of money to return to secular life. But as this matter concerns international affairs, we must publish this notice to declare it. We humbly request all officials from all walks of life to pay special attention. Sincerely, the abbot and monks of Puji, Fayu, and Huiji Temples on Putuo Mountain.

Page 9

Important News 65

From 11 p.m. to 5 a.m. the next morning, traffic was cut off. All embankment bandits were also captured, so the order was maintained stably. After the entire city was flooded, the department immediately dispatched security teams and armed police officers from the Public Security Bureau to organize patrol teams, who traveled to and from the streets in small boats, conducting strict patrols and deploying sentry posts, stationed in front of and behind the lanes, also staying in boats. If anyone was discovered taking advantage of the flood, they would be executed on the spot. At the same time, the Military Affairs Office also dispatched Deputy Officers Wang and Jiang, along with the Fourth Eighth Division military police battalion, to be stationed at the intersection of Minsheng Road and at the Zhongnan Hotel to suppress any disturbances.

Military Affairs Office Meeting: At 2 p.m. on the 2nd, Director He Chengjun convened an emergency meeting at the Military Affairs Office, attended by Xu Yuanquan, Supervisor of Bandit Suppression in the Sichuan, Hunan, and Hubei Border Areas, Xia Douyin, Garrison Commander, Qian Dajun, Fortress Commander, He Baohua, Mayor, Liu Wendao, Director of Civil Affairs, Fang Dazhi, Director of Construction, Chen Keming, Director of Water Conservancy, Su Shi’an, Director of Public Security for the Provincial Capital, and Wang Shiliu, Director of Public Security for Hankou. They decided to establish a Disaster Prevention Office to protect public order, appointing Xu Yuanquan as Supervisor and Xia Douyin as Co-Supervisor. Yang Shaodong, Chief of Staff of the Tenth Army, and Ye Peng, Chief of Staff of the Garrison Command, were responsible for the arrangements. It was also decided that the Construction Department, Water Conservancy Bureau, and Wuhan Public Security Bureau would work through the night. After the meeting, Xu and Xia conferred and decided to temporarily set up the Disaster Prevention Office within the General Chamber of Commerce, delineate disaster prevention areas, and implement emergency measures. Special attention was also given to strengthening the protection of the Zhang Gong Dyke, which had not yet collapsed.

Strict Prohibition of Price Gouging: With most shops closed due to the flooding, merchants of rice, coal, oil, and salt took the opportunity to profiteer, raising prices by more than double, causing great suffering to the refugees. The Military Affairs Office sent a letter to the Chamber of Commerce, instructing them to ensure fair prices, otherwise military law would be enforced. The letter stated, "Regarding the recent catastrophic flooding in Wuhan, a rare occurrence in sixty years, the disaster is extremely severe. Refugees from all areas have gathered in the three towns, suffering from the elements and enduring unspeakable hardships. In addition to the joint efforts of officials, merchants, and all sectors to provide relief, all merchants must consider the plight of the surviving refugees, act with conscience, and strive for fair prices to help alleviate their suffering. Therefore, we hereby request your esteemed association to inform all merchants to comply, jointly take responsibility, and avert this calamity. Anyone found taking advantage of the situation by raising prices, profiteering, hoarding goods, or deliberately creating scarcity will be dealt with according to military law without leniency."

Origin of the Disaster: This flood has not only affected Hankou but has also submerged many counties throughout the province. The main reason is that both the Yangtze and Han Rivers have risen, and downstream provinces have also experienced flooding simultaneously. The direct downpour was combined with the blockage of the drainage channels, so the situation became uncontrollable. However, according to other sources, the embezzlement of dike funds by local merchants, the lack of regular maintenance, and the official negligence and failure to carry out timely rescue efforts also seem to be contributing factors. The dike funds of Hubei Province were originally managed by a committee and were not to be used for any other purpose. However, several months ago, the committee's accountant deposited a large sum of several hundred thousand yuan with the Shifangchuanjiang Company, which was then embezzled, making it difficult to repair and strengthen the dikes. This flood had been brewing for a month, and there was ample opportunity to carry out rescue work, but due to inadequate rescue efforts, the breaches occurred. Tracing the origins, there is reason for regret. (August 3rd)

After the Chelueba Dam Was Opened, There Was Also a Lake Tsunami 66

The Hongze, Gaobao, and Shaobo Lakes All Experienced Lake Tsunamis Simultaneously

Water Levels Were Over Two Feet Higher Than the Lake Dikes, Causing Extremely Severe Disaster

Yangzhou dispatch: The previous reports have detailed the situation of the rampant Yangtze River water and the mutual dispute between the people along the river bank who were fighting over opening the dams to protect the dikes. Unexpectedly, as of the 2nd, the Yumatou water level on the canal, which serves as a standard, has reached one zhang, eight chi, and eight cun, exceeding the level of the Chelueba dam opening in the tenth year of the Republic by one chi and five cun. At that time, the number of cracks along the bank increased daily, and by 2 p.m. on that day, several dike openings had collapsed one after another. If the dam was not opened again, the counties upstream would have faced an immediate and uncontrollable disaster. Therefore, a discussion was held with the people of Xinghua and other downstream counties who were present, saying that once a breach occurred, everyone would perish together. However, the people of those areas still did not agree, and some even brought their elderly and children and lay down on the dam to show their determination to fight to the death. This continued until 4 p.m., when the southwest wind suddenly intensified, and the water from the west of the lake slammed directly against the east bank, threatening to submerge even those guarding the bank. As a result, Director Wu, Director Mao, and other officials and gentry, in consultation with the county magistrates of Xingdongtai and other counties, persuaded the people guarding the dam to disperse and carried out the digging of mud holes. Thus, the Chelueba Dam, which had been contested for half a month, was opened at 4:15 p.m. on August 2nd. As for the losses suffered by the five counties downstream, it is not possible to estimate them at this time. After the dam was opened, the counties of Jiangdu, Gaoyou, and Baoying were just beginning to feel relieved when bad news came that night (i.e., 1 a.m. on the 3rd). The four major lakes of Hongze, Gaoyou, Baoying, and Shaobo suddenly experienced lake tsunamis simultaneously, with the water exceeding the dike by more than two feet. All the surrounding polder fields were submerged by more than ten thousand mu. The disaster area reached thousands of li. All the areas bordering the provinces of Jiangsu and Anhui, such as Shui Ba Township, Miaotou Wei, Tongxing Wei, Hexing Wei, and Changchun Wei, were transformed into flooded lands in a moment. The losses of people and livestock were immense. It is truly a rare disaster not seen in seventy years.

Zhenjiang dispatch: The water level in the canal within Jiangsu Province is still increasing daily. On the 2nd of this month, the Yumatou in Gaoyou rose another four cun, reaching a total depth of one zhang, eight chi, and eight cun. Although the workers have been making great efforts to rescue and maintain the canal dikes, they are still in imminent danger. The Provincial Water Conservancy Bureau recently received a telegram stating that the commissioners, directors of the Water Conservancy Bureau, etc., appointed by the provincial government and various departments met at 4 p.m. on the 2nd with the county magistrates of Gaoxingdongtai and other four counties to persuade the people guarding the dam to disperse and release the Chelueba Dam to the sea. The water flow was immediately very smooth, and the order was still good. This time, the canal dike has been submerged for a long time, and with the scouring of the wind and waves, the dike body must be greatly damaged. After the opening of the dam, the dam bottom will be damaged by the enormous amount of water. The amount of money required for the future follow-up project is conceivable. It is said that during the great water disaster in the tenth year of the Republic, the summer flood prevention rescue and post-disaster project cost reached one million yuan. In recent years, the counties have often used various excuses to intercept the mu loss for water management, and the amount submitted to the Construction Department has been small. In the 18th year, only more than 130,000 yuan was submitted, and in the 19th year, only more than 80,000 yuan was submitted. This year, after the abolition of the li, the 10% of the goods tax levied under the various tax offices in Jiangbei for water management has no funds. With the shortage of funds, the major water management projects have not been actively carried out. The funds for the spring repair and summer prevention of the canal dike have always been paid by the province. In this time of great water disaster, the rescue project cannot be done without a large amount of money. The Finance Department has repeatedly received telegrams from the Construction Department urging payment, and it is said that it has successively allocated 30,000 yuan and is still trying to raise money to meet the urgent needs. (3rd)

The Flood in the West River of Guangdong Province is Still Serious 67

The Provincial Government Allocates Another 100,000 Yuan for Relief

Guangzhou dispatch: According to the latest investigation, the flood in Guangdong Province has been severe. All the West River basin, as well as the Beijiang River, have suffered infinite losses. At the moment, the Northern River has receded, and the Guangdong-Shaoguan Road can be normally open. However, the Western River has receded in limited amount, and the broken embankments are still a vast expanse of water. Although the highland areas have receded seven or eight feet in the past week, the upper reaches of the West River have been experiencing continuous rain in recent days, and the water level has risen. On July 28, the water in Zhaoqing Jinliwei rose eight or nine feet, and the flood was about to overflow the surface of the base. Farmers from all jurisdictions are rescuing day and night. The Jiujiang Sangyuanwei are now in imminent danger. The Guangdong Flood Relief Association has now reorganized the tenth relief team, and set off on the Guangdong-Shaoguan train on the 30th to Yingde and Qingyuan, carrying 50,000 catties of rice, medicines, and dry food. Overseas Cantonese in Shanghai have also remitted relief funds several times. Cai Chang of Dasing Company has remitted 10,000 yuan to the Cantonese Overseas Association's flood relief office and handed it over to the local Fangbian Hospital for collection. The Guangzhao Guild Hall has also remitted 30,000 yuan for relief, which was received by the water relief association on the 29th. The funds will be stored in the association and distributed separately. The government has also sent a letter from the Department of Civil Affairs to the Department of Finance to allocate another 100,000 yuan for distribution to the counties for disaster relief. The Department of Finance has allocated the full amount to the Department of Civil Affairs on the 26th, which will be distributed to the affected counties to claim for disaster relief. It is said that the Department of Civil Affairs believes that the disaster in Qingyuan County is serious. In addition to the 9,000 yuan already allocated, another 5,000 yuan has recently been allocated to provide universal relief. (July 30th)

Heavy Rain in Xuzhou Causes Flood Disaster 68

Water Depth on the Ground is Four Chi Three Cun

Xuzhou dispatch: Since the heavy rain last month, the Yellow River in the east of Xuzhou has been flooded by the sudden influx of water from the upper reaches. The houses of the residents along the river have all been submerged. By the 12th of last month, the sky began to clear. Unexpectedly, in the past two days, the weather has been abnormally hot. At 9 p.m. one evening, dark clouds gathered, followed by thunder and lightning, and heavy rain poured down all night until it stopped on the morning of the 2nd. The low-lying areas in the city and suburbs were flooded to the knees. The water in the Six Western Towns was particularly severe due to poor circulation in the northwest. The representatives of the people in the Six Western Towns, Tan Xiaochun and others, numbering more than a hundred, formed a barefooted team and went to the county government, the Bureau of Construction, the Public Security Bureau, and the First District Office to inquire about disaster relief measures. Zhu Zhengxue, Director of the Bureau of Construction, and representatives from various agencies accompanied the petitioners to inspect the water situation in the northwest. After Zhu returned, he decided to first dig a ditch behind the county government as a temporary remedy to allow the water to flow freely. As for permanent plans, no decision was made. The Yellow River water level, although it had fallen before, is now higher than before. According to the Bureau of Construction's measurement, the rainfall was 138 millimeters, an unprecedented amount. The water depth on the ground is four chi and three cun. (2nd)

Second Flood in Hefei 69

The City Walls Were Washed Away in Seven Places

Hefei County, Anhui Province, experienced a great flood a few days ago, and the city inside and outside became a flooded land. After the small weirs along the lake and river were breached, the water level had receded by more than half. Unexpectedly, from the 22nd to the 25th, there was another heavy rain, day and night, causing the water level to rise six or seven feet higher than before. The mountain torrents on the west side poured down and flowed into the city through the Shuixi Gate and the Shuiguan. The Houjie of Duancitang, Ximaqiao, Weiyaguan, Xianqiao, Wanshougong, and the Chamber of Commerce became a flooded land. The Shangjie of the Ancient Tower West Street, Shangjie Lou, Mangrenxiang, Sanfangmiao Lane, and other major streets, the shops were all submerged, and the goods were soaked, causing great losses. On the east side, the lake and river tides poured into the city through the Dongshui Gate, dividing into three branches. The north side was flooded from Dadaongmen and Mingjiao Temple to the intersection of Shizijie and the north of Guyingqiao. The south side was flooded from Xiaodongmen and Sanpailou to Xiaoshuyuan. The middle side was flooded from Feiqichi, Jiushiqiao, and Tonghefang to the entrance of Donggulou Lane. The north gate was flooded to Siwan. The streets were four or five chi deep in water, and two or three chi deep in shallower areas. The area below Mingjiao Temple was particularly deep. However, the east and west waters were only a short distance apart. On the evening of the 24th, the city wall inside the Shuixi Gate and the Shuiguan suddenly collapsed for several zhang, and the sluice gate also collapsed, causing the water to surge forward and rush in, dividing into the Gu Louqiao circle, the most prosperous Dongdajie, and rolling down. The losses to the shops here were even greater. The vegetable gardens in Jindouwei, Duanhuayuan, Miaopu, and other areas in the city were level with the rooftops and drifted away completely. Fortunately, the county government urgently compiled wooden rafts to provide relief. There were few drownings. Outside the Shuixi Gate and the North Gate, the area was tens of li wide and endless. Outside the Dadongmen, Yangmatou, Maimaijie, Baibu’an, and Sanlitan, and outside the Xiaodongmen, Dawangmiao, Wenchanggong, Wu Jiao Xiang, and Zhou Gutui, the area was tens of li wide, a vast expanse of water. The houses all collapsed, and countless people and livestock were swept away. The Dongdawei, which was previously left as a sole survivor, was also broken. It is said that more than a thousand people were drowned during the rescue. The autumn harvest of the seventy-two weirs has become a pie in the sky. According to the self-defense group's investigation, the city wall has collapsed in seven places: four places from Fangshengchi to the Shuixi Gate, two places from the Shuixi Gate to the North Gate, and one place at Dadongmen, which is about six or seven zhang in the largest extent. At the moment, traffic in the four townships and the city is blocked by water. Every family in the city has collapsed walls and houses. Many people in the four townships have taken refuge in the treetops, hills, and highlands. The wails of the homeless, foodless, and landless are deafening. Most of them have been drowned by their families. Today, Deputy Division Commander Li, County Magistrate Zhang, First District Chief Liu Mingfu, Construction Bureau Director Wu Qingquan, and various public groups have begun to survey the flooded areas in order to report to the province for disaster relief and to appeal to the overseas hometown associations and Chinese and foreign relief societies to benefit the disaster-stricken people. According to the old people, this flood is the worst since the 22nd year of Guangxu.

Donggu is Changed to Pingchi County 70

The County Seat is Located in Longnan Town

Nanchang dispatch: Donggu is located at the southernmost tip of Ji'an, about 120 li from Jicheng, straddling the border of Yongfeng, Xingguo, Jishui, Taihe, and five counties. All around, such as Longgang, Tantou, Shuinan, Chengkang, and Fulang Pit, are towering mountains and dangerous terrain. In the middle, there is the Gujiang River, which allows wooden rafts to pass through Ji'an. On both sides of the Gujiang River, there are about 300 square li of flat land, fertile fields, and residents in dozens of villages. Donggu Wei is located in the middle, with dozens of shops. During the previous Qing Dynasty, the area was also occupied by thieves, who killed and robbed, and the government could do nothing about it. In the sixteenth year of the Republic, the Communist Zeng Tianyu occupied Wan'an, and the local bandits responded one after another. Donggu then fell into the hands of the red bandits. Zhu Mao also used it as a base, setting up a false peasant-worker revolutionary committee, the Gannan Special Committee, a military committee, the Jiangxi Soviet government peasant-worker bank, and a military political school. Last November, the counties along the Ganjiang River, such as Qingjiang, Xingan, Xiajiang, Jishui, and Ji'an, were successively recovered by the government forces. Subsequently, the Gong and Luo divisions met in Donggu from Ji'an and Taihe, with the 18th Division of Zhang Huizan stationed there. Zhang then submitted a petition to the provincial government, stating that Donggu was too far from the county seats of the five counties, making it difficult to control, so the red bandits were able to calmly occupy it and grow slowly. If it is desired to thoroughly eliminate them, the county seat should be re-established with Donggu as the center, and the Wende and Zhegui townships of Jishui, the Mingde township of Yongfeng, the Chunhua of Ji'an, the Xiancha of Taihe, and the Fengbian Baishichenggang of Xingguo should all belong to it. However, the provincial government only designated Donggu as a special administrative region due to the shortage of administrative expenses and appointed Xu Wenming as the commissioner of the region. Later, Donggu was again captured by bandits on New Year's Day this year, Zhang Shichang was killed in battle, and the administrative commissioner set up an office in Ji'an. It was not until the 27th of last month that Donggu was recovered by the government forces for the second time. The current party and government committee, in order to make the Gan people forever cherish their great achievements and forever be afraid of the red disaster, has decided to establish a county seat in Donggu to prepare for local rehabilitation in order to permanently eliminate the bandit roots. It is also said that it has been named Pingchi County, and the county seat is located in Longnan Town, 20 li east of Donggu, with jurisdiction over all of Ji'an County east of the Ganjiang River (from Yonghe Yangtian Xin'an Futian to Donggu), the Zhangjiadu, Shuinan, Baisha, and Beihu lines south of Jishui County, and the western part of Yongfeng County including Shaxi Hanxia, Junbu, and Nankeng. The committee is still awaiting consultation with the counties to determine the detailed boundaries. As for the candidate for the county committee chairman, Li Baozhong has been announced as the appointee. Li is a graduate of the Baoding Military Academy and is now

Zhu Mao's Remnant Bandits Plot to Flee to Western Jiangxi 71

They Already Show Signs of Abandoning Ruijin

Nanchang dispatch: After the bandit suppression army recovered Donggu, Zhu Mao, Peng, Huang, and other bandits fled from Xingguo and Yudu to Ruijin. General Commander Jiang immediately ordered the various armies to attack Xingguo, Yudu, and Ruijin. Yesterday, on the 30th, they broke through Fangshiling, which connected Donggu and Xingguo, and captured and disarmed the remnants of Huang Gonglue's troops, numbering about 2,000, with about 1,600 guns. The city of Xingguo will also be taken in a matter of days. However, the Military Affairs Office recently received a reconnaissance report from an aircraft that the bandits who had fled from Donggu to Ruijin have recently moved west from Jiubao (about dozens of li west of Ruijin). All the bandits in Yudu and Xingguo have the potential to cross the Ganjiang River through Taihe and Wan'an and flee to western Jiangxi and eastern Hunan. The red bandits in Ruijin are only a small number of peasant bandits. Their main force is gathered between Yudu and Xingguo and is advancing westward very quickly. After receiving the report, General Commander Jiang immediately ordered the various armies to separately encircle and pursue the bandits from Xingguo and Yudu, and to deploy along the Ganjiang River to block their passage and prevent them from crossing the river. (2nd)

Hunanese Organize

National Group for Purchasing and Using Domestic Goods 72

Every Ten People Form a Group to Mutually Help Each Other Purchase and Use Domestic Goods

Changsha dispatch: After the Korean Massacre, people in various places spontaneously organized Anti-Japanese and Aid-Korea Associations or Foreign Affairs Support Associations to serve as a support for the government and seek diplomatic victory. The people of Hunan Province had already organized an Anti-Japanese and Aid-Korea Association. Now, in order to achieve universal and permanent benefits through economic severance, they have initiated the organization of a "National Group for Purchasing and Using Domestic Goods." Every ten people form a group to mutually supervise, persuade, and prohibit the use of foreign goods and purchase and use domestic goods. Those who violate this will be severely punished in order to achieve broad and powerful results. The organizational rules were drafted into twelve articles by the Provincial Party Affairs Steering Committee yesterday and submitted to the joint meeting of the Party and government on July 31. They were passed and promulgated as an order to all levels of party departments, all agencies, all county governments, and all groups to comply with the organization. The rules of the Hunan Provincial National Group for Purchasing and Using Domestic Goods, passed by the joint meeting of the Party and government, are recorded below. Article 1: These rules are specifically formulated to promote and implement the purchase and use of domestic goods. Article 2: The responsibilities of this group, in addition to publicizing and introducing the purchase of domestic goods, do not include other political functions. Article 3: All members of this group must uniformly prohibit the use of foreign goods (existing goods must be registered in advance and can still be used), but items necessary for scientific or medical purposes are exempt from this restriction if approved by more than half of the members of this group. Article 4: This group shall consist of three or five comrades from the branch of the Chinese Kuomintang as basic members, and then five or seven members of the public shall be persuaded by the basic members to organize it. The aforementioned basic members shall be compiled and notified by the executive committee of the branch for implementation. Article 5: This group shall have one director, who shall be elected by the members in rotation for a term of three months and shall not be re-elected. Article 6: The director of this group must convene the members once a month to discuss the various matters of the group. If necessary, a temporary meeting may be convened. Article 7: When this group is formed, an oath ceremony must be held and reported to the local party department, which will send personnel to participate. Article 8: The members of this group have the obligation to mutually persuade and admonish each other to fulfill the purpose of this group. If they disobey the persuasion and deliberately violate the purpose of this group, they may report to the director and convene a meeting for discussion. Article 9: Every six months, this group shall report the situation of purchasing and using domestic goods to the directly subordinate branch for record. Article 10: People in various places may freely organize implementation groups for purchasing and using domestic goods in accordance with the provisions of these rules, but they should be guided by the local party department. Article 11: This group shall advocate domestic goods and may request party departments at all levels to investigate domestic products, set up domestic goods markets, and assume all other guidance and introduction responsibilities in conjunction with the government. Article 12: These rules shall be implemented from the date of promulgation by the Provincial Party Affairs Steering Committee and shall be submitted to the Central Training Department for record. (31st)

Wang Chia-chen's Talk Upon Passing Through Qingdao 73

Qingdao Dispatch: Wang Chia-chen, Vice Minister of Foreign Affairs, arrived in Qingdao on the Dalian Maru from Shanghai on July 31st. This morning (the 2nd) at 7:00 AM, he took the Jiaoji Railway train to Jinan and then to Peiping. According to Wang's conversation with reporters, his mission in going north is to attend the International League of Nations conference in Geneva, and to visit Deputy Commander Zhang in Peiping to make some reports. Regarding the case of the Korean riot and the massacre of overseas Chinese, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs has lodged a serious protest with Japan. However, the Japanese side, seeing the unrest in China and the inability to unite externally, is purely adopting a delaying tactic to wait for changes in the situation. If our country wants to win the negotiation, we must first quell the internal strife, and then unite from top to bottom, so that the Japanese have no opportunity to take advantage of, and this case will be easily resolved. As for the large amount of property of overseas Chinese in Korea, the returning overseas Chinese should still return to Korea to manage it and await a resolution from both sides. Furthermore, Shi Yousan's army is already surrounded on all sides, with the front line near Shijiazhuang, and it is expected to be resolved soon. (August 2nd)

Bengbu Citizens Hold Anti-Japanese Rally 74

Jointly Discuss Implementing a Boycott of Japanese Goods

Bengbu Dispatch: All circles in Bengbu are deeply indignant about the Wanbaoshan incident and the massacre of overseas Chinese by Koreans. Representatives from various agencies and trade associations held a meeting at the District Party Headquarters at 3:00 PM on the 2nd to discuss ways to proceed. More than 40 people attended that day and resolved: (1) To immediately establish a Preparatory Office for the Bengbu Anti-Japanese Aid Overseas Chinese Citizens' Assembly; (2) To assign the Public Security Bureau, the Chamber of Commerce, and the District Party Headquarters to be responsible for preparations; (3) The Preparatory Office organization will be divided into three departments: General Affairs, Propaganda, and Discipline; (4) The General Affairs Department will be undertaken by the Chamber of Commerce, the Propaganda Department will be undertaken by the District Party Headquarters, and the Discipline Department will be jointly undertaken by the Finance Ministry's Tax Police Special Task Force, the Bengbu Public Security Bureau, and the Changhuai Water Police Bureau; (5) The preparatory expenses are set at 180 yuan, which will be distributed among various agencies, groups, and banks; (6) It is scheduled to be held on August 6th at 8:00 AM on a platform built in the open space north of the Heng Railway. If it rains, it will be changed to the Commercial and People's Stage; (7) The Preparatory Office will work at the District Party Headquarters. The meeting adjourned at 5:00 PM. As for boycotting Japanese goods, it must wait until the Citizens' Assembly is held to propose a vote and then implement it. (August 2nd)

The Progress of the Anti-Japanese Movement in Fuzhou 75

Fuzhou Dispatch: All circles in Fuzhou have recently felt unusually indignant about the Japanese atrocities in Wanbaoshan and various parts of Korea. On July 23rd, the Minhou County Party Headquarters convened representatives of various groups to hold a joint meeting, and it was resolved to organize the Fujian Provincial Capital All Circles Anti-Japanese Association. The Provincial Party Headquarters, the County Party Headquarters, the Minguo Daily, the Dongfang Daily, the Seamen's Union, the Yangwu Workers' Union, the Promote National Goods Association, the Women's Relief Association, the County Chamber of Commerce, the Provincial Fuzhou High School, and the County Minhou Junior High School were selected as committee members. On the 25th, the first committee meeting was held, and it was resolved to organize the method. There will be three standing committee members and four sections: General Affairs, Propaganda, Investigation, and Registration. On the 27th, the second committee meeting was held, and the Provincial Party Headquarters, the County Party Headquarters, and the County Chamber of Commerce were elected as standing committee members, and they began working immediately. The association has now resolved to stop the import of Japanese goods starting from August 6th, and at the same time notify various merchant guilds to investigate the current inventory of goods in the shops within the guild and register with the association, with a deadline for auctioning and clearing them. It also sent letters to the Lianjiang, Changle, Fuqing, Xiapu, and Ningde coastal county party headquarters to unanimously rise up, lead the people, organize anti-Japanese associations, and investigate and prohibit the smuggling of Japanese goods into the interior. The Minhou County Chamber of Commerce also convened representatives from various trade associations on the 29th to discuss ways to stop the transportation of new goods and clear old goods. Therefore, the anti-Japanese atmosphere in Minyuan has been quite tense recently. However, the provincial government believes that during this period of bandit suppression and martial law, local order is extremely important, and it is sincerely afraid that bad elements will infiltrate and use foreign affairs issues to disrupt public security. Therefore, on the 28th, it specially sent Zhang Jingtang, the section chief of the Second Section, to the Provincial Party Headquarters to discuss solutions with Secretary Zhan Rufang, and three items were formulated: (1) Anti-Japanese movements in various places should be led by the Party Headquarters; (2) The boycott of Japanese goods should be handled with caution; (3) The name must be changed to the Foreign Affairs Support Association. (July 30th)

The Bandit Disaster in Fujian Province Urgently Needs Relief 76

Fuzhou Dispatch: The Fujian Provincial Government has set up a Red Area Relief Association because of the severe disaster situation in the red disaster areas in the past. It has also organized a fundraising team. The association has now formulated a disaster situation survey form and distributed it to the counties that have been affected by bandits for investigation and reporting to the association, so that it can be distributed for relief separately. In addition, because the disaster situation is serious and fundraising is delayed, it is not enough to meet the urgent need. The Provincial Relief Committee also sent a telegram to the Central Relief Committee, saying: "The Red Bandits in Jiangxi Province were attacked by the Central Army and fled into Fujian. The counties of Minbei, Jianning, Taining, Shaowu, Guangze, Chong'an, and Jiangle have successively fallen, and they have committed arson, murder, rape, and looting, which is inhumane. We have previously telegraphed to request the allocation of huge funds to provide relief. We have also received a reply stating that we will discuss the allocation of relief funds after they have been raised. We have seen that your association cares about the people of Nanzhou and the coastal disaster victims, and we all sincerely wish you well. Now, the bandits have retreated from Minbei to Minxi, and Changting, Shanghang, Liancheng, and Ninghua have successively reported alarms, and the local area is in a state of disarray, and people are displaced everywhere. We urgently present our words and await your telegram." (July 30th)

The Shantou Case of Vengeful Ghosts 77

Anecdotes of the Independent Second Division Interrogating Vengeful Ghosts

A Three-Year-Old Murder for Money Case is Cleared

Modern Spiritualists Should Study This

Shantou Dispatch: Liu Donghai, a soldier in the Seventh Company of the Second Battalion of the Teaching Regiment under Zhang Ruigui of the Independent Second Division stationed in Shantou, recently suffered from severe muscle cramps in both knees. The bones in his lower legs were extremely painful, and his skin was blue and black, as if he had been beaten. He could not move. Zeng Ruisheng, the company commander, sent Liu to the health team for treatment. In the ward, Liu often felt haunted by ghosts at night, and his chest often felt oppressed by heavy objects, making it difficult for him to move freely, and he felt suffocated. Liu suspected that he was being haunted by demons and did not want to stay in the team, so he moved back to the company headquarters. After arriving at the company headquarters, although there were many soldiers living together, the haunting continued as before. After Liu fell asleep, it was as if someone stuffed his mouth with a face towel, or as if his hands were tied behind his back with iron wire. He often stared straight ahead and muttered to himself. Wang Xinfa, the squad leader, saw this strange situation and always woke him up. The soldiers in the same company also saw it several times. Therefore, the story of ghosts haunting the company spread throughout the army.

Company Commander Zeng Ruisheng has always prided himself on being upright, loyal, and brave. He has fought on the battlefield and camped in ancient temples in the wilderness and never believed that there were ghosts and monsters in the world. One night, he saw Liu's strange condition in the company headquarters and became curious. He jokingly wrote a text to summon the ghost to make a decision. He drafted a few lines, and just as he was about to light incense and burn it, Liu Donghai suddenly began to rave in his sleep, his voice and accent completely different from usual. Zeng quickly ordered the scribe to record what Liu said in his dream in writing to get to the bottom of it.

Liu was originally from Qinlian, Guangdong Province. In his dream, he suddenly spoke in the local Guangxi dialect: "Speak! Won't you tell me about your evil deeds? It doesn't matter if you beat me to death. You also beat my brother and his wife to death. I will tie you up every night!" Company Commander Zeng was also horrified when he heard this and asked, "Who are you? What grievances do you have?" The ghost attached to Liu's body replied, "I am from Bobai County, Guangxi. What is your name?" He replied, "My surname is Liao, and my name is Kun, the Kun next to the fire character. My brother's name is Liao Qi." He asked what he did for a living, and he replied, "I do small business." He asked how many people were killed in his family, and he replied, "Two brothers and a new wife who was pregnant. I have been following him for three years. That day, I hit him with a stick, and he couldn't move anymore. After he killed us, he changed his name. There is also a military ticket. If you don't believe me, look at it." As he spoke, Liu unconsciously untied the leather bag on his waistband in his dream. Company Commander Zeng took the bag and opened it. Inside, there was a cloth collar badge of Wu Qihua, and a ticket with his name written on it.

Company Commander Zeng immediately promised to avenge Er's grievances, and Liu fell silent and snored like thunder. After a while, Liu woke up, and Company Commander Zeng asked him about what he said in his dream. Liu was stunned and didn't know. Zeng showed Liu what the scribe had recorded, and he lowered his head and said nothing. He confessed that three years ago, when he was the squad leader in Fan Dexing's regiment, his original name was Wu Qihua. He set out from Bobai County. One day, when he was on sentry duty at the junction of Hepu County, he saw two men with the surname Liao on the road, followed by a new wife, carrying 400 yuan in silver dollars. He immediately used the bayonet on his gun to stab the three of them to death and robbed them of the cash. The accomplices who committed the crime with him that day were still soldiers. Company Commander Zeng found out the truth. The petition for vengeance by the wronged soul has been confessed by Liu Donghai himself and cannot be disbelieved. He reported the details of that night and the sick soldier's confession to the battalion commander of the teaching regiment, who forwarded it to the division commander Zhang Ruigui, requesting that Liu Donghai, who had changed his name to Wu Qihua, be punished according to the law to uphold the law and comfort the wronged soul. At the same time, the division headquarters sent a letter to Bobai County, Guangxi, to investigate the truth of the matter three years ago, pending a final decision. (July 31st)

Changshu 83

The Adjudication of Party Cases Does Not Need to Be Transferred for Jurisdiction: Shi Minyong, the current Supervisory Committee Member of the County Party Headquarters, was accused by Tong Shizhong, a party member from Meili, of fraud. The Haiyu Daily, which published the truth of the case, was also attached. After receiving the complaint, the County Government approved "Wait for the summons to be verified." However, more than half a month has passed, and no summons has been issued. People in the community are paying attention. It is learned that County Magistrate Tan Yigui saw that although he had approved the summons, the complainant was a member of the Party Headquarters. Although the party and government organs were not subordinate to each other, the committee member and the county magistrate met every day in the same area. No matter how fair the case is handled in the future, there may be controversy from the outside world. Therefore, he voluntarily applied to the High Court for recusal and requested a transfer of jurisdiction. Yesterday, it was heard that the High Court had ruled that the Party Headquarters was not an agency under the County Government and that the Party Committee was not a civil servant. Therefore, there was no need for recusal, and the case could be handled according to law without transferring jurisdiction. It is said that the County Government will schedule a summons soon.

The Case of the Former County Magistrate Embezzling Funds Will Be Summoned Soon: Chen Meisheng, a local resident, because Zhuang Yan, the father of Zhuang Huaguang, the current Director of the County Finance Bureau, was suspected of embezzling a large amount of money during his tenure in Changshu, and the amount that has been found is already more than 11,000 yuan. He has requested the Supervisory Yuan, the Department of Finance, and the Suzhou High Court Procuratorate to investigate and pursue the matter according to the law and recover the embezzled funds. The Suzhou High Court Procuratorate has issued an order to the county, ordering it to investigate and handle the case according to the law. The County Government intends to schedule a summons for the plaintiff in accordance with the Criminal Procedure Law to clarify the truth.

Construction Workers Will Sue the County Government: The County Government, in order to build a new prison, contracted with Gong Fengji for a bid of 21,000 yuan. It was to be built in accordance with the bidding regulations and construction details. However, there was an existing river pool on the site that had to be filled before a house could be built on it. This filling work and the piles were not specified in the regulations. Gong Fengji said that the bid price was already low, and requested that the County Government slightly subsidize the pool work materials that were not included. The County Government refused. Gong was unable to construct due to difficulties, so he applied to the county to withdraw the bid. The County Government ordered the second lowest bidder, Wu Zhongji, to undertake the construction, and fined Gong Fengji 120 yuan for delaying the project. Gong believed that the reason for withdrawing the bid was entirely due to errors in the regulations and had nothing to do with him. He refused to pay the fine. The County Government ordered the bailiffs to collect the fine within a time limit, otherwise he would be detained. Gong had no choice but to pay the 120 yuan to the County Government. At the same time, he filed an appeal with the Department of Civil Affairs, arguing that the County Government had subsidized Wu Zhongji's labor and materials and that the treatment was different.

The Party Headquarters' Election of Provincial Representatives Failed: The County Party Headquarters elected provincial representatives. Earlier, each district elected 21 preliminary election representatives. On August 1st, a second election was held at the County Party Headquarters. Chen Kanghe was dispatched by the province to Changshu to supervise. By the afternoon, only ten people attended, which was less than the legal number and could not hold the meeting. At around 4:00 PM, 18 people arrived. At that time, the County Party Headquarters feared that the violence that occurred at the election of representatives last year would be repeated. Therefore, it posted a notice at the door stating that only preliminary election representatives and staff members attending the meeting were allowed to enter. It also ordered the Public Security Bureau to dispatch more police officers to guard the door, which was very strict. Unexpectedly, at 4:20 PM, just as the meeting was about to begin, Chen Kanghe, the provincial supervisor, suddenly became ill, vomiting a lot, and announced the adjournment of the meeting. He was immediately sent to Changshu Hospital for treatment. According to Director Gu, it was likely acute gastroenteritis and he would not recover in a day or two.

Zhenjiang 84

The Gaozi Security Corps Fiercely Fights Bandits: The mountainous areas of Gaozi in the western countryside have always been areas where bandits come and go. The Security Office previously sent a team to search and suppress them, and a tip-off led to the arrest of bandit leader Chen Wenqi in Hangzhou, who was executed by firing squad. The people began to feel more at ease. However, although Chen was executed, dozens of Chen's followers still had guns that had not been seized. At around 9:00 AM yesterday morning, they took advantage of the redeployment of the troops stationed there and gathered dozens of people to attack the Tanggang Security Corps in an attempt to seize their weapons. Fortunately, the security corps had been prepared in advance. After the bandits arrived, they fought bravely and fiercely. Three bandits were killed. The bandits were unable to resist and began to flee. Tong Jiasheng, the district chief of the area, is still afraid that the bandits will return and has telegraphed the County Government to request the Security Office to immediately send a team to search and suppress them to maintain security.

The Civil Affairs and Education Departments Should Distribute Ma Yuren's Ill-Gotten Gains: The Department of Civil Affairs and the Department of Education recently received an order from the Provincial Government to order them to jointly dispose of Ma Yuren's ill-gotten gains in Yancheng and Funing counties in accordance with the revised regulations on the disposal of ill-gotten gains and to report the matter. It was decided that the portion of the ill-gotten gains of the traitor in Yancheng and Funing counties belonging to the province should be estimated according to the original register, totaling 317,801 yuan. According to Article 9 of the revised regulations on the disposal of ill-gotten gains, the ill-gotten gains should be distributed between the education and relief departments. The education portion should be divided into various assets, estimated according to the original estimate, totaling 158,896 yuan. The relief portion should be divided into various assets, estimated according to the original estimate, totaling 158,905 yuan. They were jointly negotiated and finalized and reported to the Provincial Government for record.

Nantong 85

Measures to Prevent Bandits Along the Coast of Northern Jiangsu: Bandits often harass the coastal areas of Northern Jiangsu. In addition to assigning Shen Fengsan's maritime guerrilla team, which was reorganized by the Provincial Security Office, to the Yancheng and Funing areas to patrol the sea and arrest pirates, the Provincial Security Office ordered the Tongtai counties to quickly form water patrol teams and to reorganize the existing fishing groups in various fields. The coastal transportation will use the old Fan Causeway to expand and build a highway for automobiles. It will be implemented after the Provincial Government's Pacification Supervisor approves it.

Nantong, Jiangyin, and Changshu Counties Jointly Maintain the Sandbar: Liuhai Sandbar, which is jointly governed by Nantong, Jiangyin, and Changshu counties, is collapsing severely. The Department of Construction has ordered the three counties to jointly carry out sandbar maintenance projects. The plan has been formulated. The county magistrates, directors of the construction bureaus, and local representatives of the three counties will meet on the sandbar on the 6th to discuss the progress.

The Slaughter Industry Continues to Strike: The slaughter industry in Nantong is protesting against the new tax increase imposed by Xu Jingqing and has gone on strike. There is still no solution, and the stalemate continues.

Gaoyou 86

Bandits in Panjiaxia Shot and Killed Four Militia Members: Yao Jiashen, the head of the Panjiaxia Militia in the third district of the county, led farmers to build dikes the night before. Guo Wenlin, the platoon leader of the security corps, led militia members to maintain order on the site. At that time, two bandit boats happened to pass by, carrying more than ten bandits. Platoon Leader Guo immediately ordered them to stop the boat for inspection. Unexpectedly, the bandits suddenly opened fire and shot and killed four militia members on the spot: Cai Jinshou, Xu Zhibu, Guo Weixin, and Chen Daying. They then roared away. Yao Tuandong has reported to the County Government and requested strict arrest.

Pinghu 87

Huzhi, a Property Broker, Was Interrogated by the County: Ma Xianghe, an old farmer from Nan Village, Xinmiao, sold 180 dan of leased land for the Zhu family on Xueqian Street in the city last winter. It was then purchased by the bandit leader Zhu Luo Amei through various people at 44 yuan per dan. Ma Xianghe acted as the middleman. Later, when he learned that it was purchased by Zhu Luo Amei, he was afraid of being discovered and fled in fear of being punished. Now that the bandit leader has been executed for a long time, he has sneaked back to his village. Yesterday, he and his son A'da went to Yazhen Town to shop and were secretly reported to the army. The two Mas were arrested on the spot and taken to the county. Yesterday, Song, the trial officer of the County Government, opened a court for interrogation. Ma Xianghe confessed that he did not know the bandit Zhu Luo Amei and that Zhu, the accountant of the Zhu family, had mentioned in a teahouse in Xinmiao Town that he was eager to sell. He was motivated by greed and was willing to act as an intermediary. Later, Zhu's accountant gave him 40 yuan as a brokerage fee. All the land sales accounts were also transferred to him. His son Ma A'da confessed that he was not involved in the sale of land and did not receive any silver dollars. This time, he went shopping with his father in Yaqian and was arrested. Trial Officer Song ordered that the Zhu family and the accountant be summoned to the county for further interrogation. The two defendants were returned to custody.

Hangzhou 88

The Hanghai Seawall Suddenly Subsides: The Zhejiang Construction Department received a telegram from the Provincial Government, stating that Xu Luqiao of Shili Village, Haining, reported that the Mipanxi seawall in the fourth district of the Hanghai section had subsided and was in danger. It should strictly order the project personnel of the Qiantang River Bank Project to pay attention to the protection at all times and to quickly find a way to hire workers to repair it to avoid accidents.

Young Couple Commit Suicide by Poisoning: Chen Xiaoxia, a 23-year-old resident of Dashi Port, Zhuantang, Shangsi Township, Hang County, was a teacher in a rural primary school. Last spring, he married Shen Xiaxuan, the daughter of a certain Guotang line in Jiangan. Since their marriage, their feelings have been very deep. However, because he has been unemployed for a long time, his daily expenses are high. At first, he was supported by relatives and friends, but then he could not borrow money. He became tired of the world. The night before, he took advantage of the fact that no one was prepared and drank sleeping pills with his wife at the same time, hugged each other and went to sleep. At 9:00 AM the next morning, Chen's mother saw that the sun was high in the sky and that her children had not gotten up yet. She entered the room to check and saw her children sleeping together, their faces pale. There were two empty bottles on the table. Knowing that something was wrong, she quickly called the neighbors to gather two doors and carried them to Liuhe Hospital at the gate for treatment. However, the poisoning was already deep. When they were carried to the Sanfuren Temple in Xucun, they were both dead.

The Case of Murdering a Widow Aunt and Leading a Child Is Judged: Guo Qianshun and Yishun, two brothers from Ximuzhen, Henan, Xiaofeng, had more than 10,000 gold in property left after their uncle's death, which was exclusively obtained by the widow aunt, Lizi Deshun. In February of this year, they took the opportunity to push Deshun, who had been stabbed, into the creek while they were in the field, causing her death. The county sentenced each of them to 12 years in prison. The prisoners refused to accept the sentence and appealed to the province. After many hearings by Chen, the trial judge, it was announced yesterday that Guo Qianshun was found guilty of premeditated murder and sentenced to 15 years in prison. Guo Yishun was found guilty of joint murder and the original sentence was upheld.

Part of the Hangchang Highway Is Interrupted: After the Hangchang Highway reopened the day before yesterday, business increased suddenly. However, because the Benyan for protecting farmland near Liangzhu was not removed, passengers had to get off the bus and walk for about a mile to change cars. The road from Huzhou to Yangjiabu and Changxing was about ten miles long and was flooded by seven or eight feet of water, so deep that the bottom could not be seen. Traffic was cut off. It is reported that salt and other goods in Changxing city have been exhausted, and the people are quite panicked. It is expected that the resumption of car traffic will be after one month.

Ningbo 89

Zhou Yecun Village Chief Kidnapped: Yesterday at midnight, more than ten bandits suddenly broke into the residence of Ye Weirong, the village chief of Zhou Yecun Village in Yiyao Hushan. They went straight into the bedroom, kidnapped Ye, and fired shots into the air as a warning before leaving. By the time the security team received the report and dispatched troops to pursue them, the bandits and the hostage had disappeared without a trace.

Party Committee Member Beaten and Injured by Soldiers: Zhang Changchen and Pan Nai'en, two executive committee members of the Xiangshan County Party Department, were cooling off in front of the party department at around 8:00 PM yesterday when Mao, a squad leader of the garrison team stationed in Xiangshan, suddenly led five or six soldiers to forcibly drag Zhang and Pan away. Near Jingtang Bridge, Mao pushed Zhang into the stream and threw large stones at him, causing serious head and limb injuries to Zhang. Pan was dragged to the team headquarters in the City God Temple, falsely accused of being a communist, and severely beaten. Pan suffered serious internal injuries to his head and waist. Afterwards, Zhang and Pan went to the county to have their injuries examined. Subsequently, the company commander of the team went to the county to express his condolences to Zhang and Pan. An urgent meeting was convened in the county government, and the results of the discussion were: (1) Squad leader Mao, who caused the disturbance, was sent to the county government for punishment; (2) The party committee was compensated for clothing and medical expenses; (3) Cannons were fired and a banquet was held to appease the party department. The party department was satisfied and dropped the matter.

Shaoxing 90

Foil Shops Sever Ties with Shanghai Shops Due to Tax Issues: Since the Shaoxing Foil Tax Bureau took over, the tax rates for various types of foil have been determined by the industry association and submitted to the tax collection bureau for approval. However, the Shanghai foil industry has raised objections to these tax rates, deducting nine or six cents per piece for tax and 4.8 cents for customs duties. Previously, Shaoxing appointed representatives, including Fu Xiao, and five others to go to Shanghai for negotiations, but the Shanghai shops insisted on the deductions, and no results were achieved. As this concerns the cost of materials, a meeting was convened yesterday, and it was generally agreed that the Shanghai shops were unreasonably coercing and deducting taxes, making trade difficult. It was decided that all members would temporarily sever ties with the Shanghai shops. Fearing that some might privately resume trade during the suspension period, twenty foil shops, including Zhen Chang, Cheng Tai, and Chang Chang, have sent letters to the Foil Tax Bureau requesting that the shipment of Shanghai foil pieces be suspended for tax reporting in order to find a satisfactory solution.

Anqing 91

New Resolution to the Anhui Province Reclamation Dispute: The land reclamation dispute in Anhui Province has been unresolved for over a year. The point of contention is whether the authority to reclaim land belongs to the Ministry of Finance or the provincial government. A month ago, the provincial government resolved to have the finance and construction departments, together with the director of the land reclamation bureau appointed by the ministry, draft measures to resolve the dispute. The departments and bureau immediately drafted eight measures and submitted them to the provincial government. The provincial government passed them at a standing committee meeting. The following is an excerpt of the measures: (1) Official properties and wasteland in Anhui Province, with the exception of those used by the military, camps, horses, schools, prisons, and those previously occupied or designated for use by provincial, municipal, and county departments, or those owned by government offices and houses under long-term rent collection, as well as pastures designated by the provincial government, shall be handled by the Official Property Reclamation Bureau, with the assistance of the county governments. (2) The county magistrates of each county shall, in accordance with the regulations of the Ministry, be appointed by the Official Property Reclamation Bureau in conjunction with the Finance Department to jointly manage the sub-bureaus. (3) The files of official wasteland previously received and kept by the counties shall be transferred to the official property sub-bureaus of each county by order of the Department of Civil Affairs. Those stored in the departments may be transferred at any time by official letter. (4) The examination and implementation of tax increases in each county shall be carried out in accordance with the tax increase regulations. (5) Land deeds for official wasteland that have been issued in the past shall remain valid. Those whose prices have not been cleared shall continue to be cleared by the province. (6) Land related to water conservancy shall be surveyed and managed by the Official Property Bureau in conjunction with the competent authorities. (7) The income of the Official Property Bureau shall be reported to the Ministry and the provincial government for record each month. (8) These measures shall be resolved by the provincial government and reported to the Official Property Bureau for filing with the Ministry.

Hefei 92

Notes on the Interrogation of the Bone Theft Case: Although the Public Security Bureau has cracked down on the bone theft organization and captured the sorcerer, cases of bone theft in the four villages surrounding the city continue to occur several times a day, too numerous to record. On the 22nd, Yang Qiyou from Fengtai was caught by farmers stealing bones in Chen Henggang, Shuangdunji, in the northern countryside. He was handed over to the regimental bureau and transferred to the county. This afternoon, Section Chief She interrogated him. He confessed that he and eight accomplices stole bones from Shoujing and came to Hefei to work, specializing in stealing yellow and white bones and transporting them to Shanghai to sell to foreigners at a high price. After the interrogation, he was imprisoned. Regarding the old sorcerer, who is the focus of attention in this case throughout the county, this morning, Director Wang of the 46th Division Military Law Office, at the request of various public groups, interrogated the sorcerer Hu Youzhi, Zu Muheng, Shan Guoshi, Guo Nv, the landlord surnamed Lu, and Wu Jing, the person who introduced the rental of the house, all day long. Because onlookers were not allowed, the truth is unclear. However, the first district offices of various public groups have all held meetings and decided to petition for strict punishment of the sorcerer and the landlord.

Bengbu 93

Banditry Resurges in Sixian County: Sixian County in northern Anhui has always been a gathering area. In recent years, arson, murder, robbery, and kidnapping have caused great harm to the local area. Since the major bandits Wang Kunlun, San Mao Hou, and Zhou Hanzi were successively brought to justice, banditry had subsided, and the area had gained some peace. However, recently, a large group of bandits, numbering over two hundred, has suddenly appeared in the Xin'an area of the county, entrenched in Kuangjiawa, Wushankou, and other places. They are well-armed and extremely rampant. The bandit leader, Zhou Jiu, the younger brother of Zhou Hanzi, declared that he would attack the villages and fortresses north of the county to avenge his brother. The village chiefs of the eighth district believe that with the autumn harvest season approaching, if they do not quickly suppress the bandits, the situation will spread and become difficult to control. They have now requested troops from the county government to suppress them.

National Central University Still Has 94

Hope of Establishing a Mongolian-Tibetan Class 95

In order to promote Mongolian-Tibetan education, the Ministry of Education, in addition to planning to request the Executive Yuan to allocate funds for printing teaching materials in both Manchu and Chinese to facilitate the implementation of Mongolian-Tibetan education, and in order to improve the level of education for those who intend to become teachers of Mongolian-Tibetan, the Central University was ordered to establish a Mongolian-Tibetan class. The president of the university requested a temporary postponement of the establishment of the class due to financial difficulties. It is reported that the Ministry of Education considers the establishment of the Mongolian-Tibetan class to be a matter of urgency and that it cannot be delayed. It plans to order the university to allocate funds from its special expenses to meet the needs.

New Developments at Zhejiang University 96

The Zhijiang College of Arts and Sciences (formerly Zhijiang University) at Erlongtou, Zhakou, Hangzhou, has a picturesque landscape with mountains in the background and water in front. The school's facilities, such as the dormitories for male and female students, are exquisite and elegant. The classrooms have ample air and light. The sports field, swimming pool, and gymnasium are all well-equipped. Currently, a library and a science hall are being added, both of which will be completed in the autumn semester. The library is located on the Erlongtou mountain range, looking east to Liuhe Pagoda, west to Wuyun Mountain, south to the winding Qiantang River, and north to the towering Qinwang Mountain. The beautiful scenery will be the center of the school. When the project is completed in the future, it will surely be a famous scenic spot in Zhejiang, not just an academic repository. The science hall is also quite magnificent. The first floor is a chemistry lab, the second floor is an engineering lab, and the third floor is a physics and biology lab. Its location is between Severance Hall and West Hall, which is very convenient for students to travel back and forth. The school not only strives for development in material facilities but also strives to enrich the faculty. Many well-known professors have been newly hired. In the liberal arts department, the Chinese Literature Department originally had Zhong Zhongshan and Xia Cheng Chan, both well-known scholars in the field of Chinese studies. Now, Li Yan, the former Chinese professor and chairman of the Chinese Department at Xiamen University and National Wuchang University, has been added. The Economics Department originally had Li Pei'en and Hu Jiyuan. Now, Tang Qingyong, the former professor of commerce at Daxia University and Jiaotong University, has been added. The Political Science Department has newly hired Dr. Lin Die, a professor at the University of Hawaii. The Education Department has added Xiong Wenmin, the section chief of the First Section of the Zhejiang Education Department, as a part-time professor. In the science department, the Physics Department has newly hired Yang Long, a doctor of science from the University of Nancy, France. The Chemistry Department has added Jacob Xia, the chairman of the Chemistry Department at Washington and Lee University in the United States. Dr. Xia has a long-standing reputation in the American academic community and is an authority in the world of chemistry. It is said that he was recruited to China because his son, Xia Keqin, is the chairman of the Chemistry Department at Zhijiang University. In addition, professors of English and engineering are being added. Most of the school's professors are full-time and live on campus, seeing students day and night, which has a familial spirit and greatly benefits students' studies and conduct. It is reported that the school's registration was approved by the Ministry of Education last month.

Graduates from Yangzhong, Jiangsu Province

Number of Students Admitted to National Central University and Wuhan University 97

National Central University: 54 students, Wuhan University: 10 students, Zhejiang University: 10 students

In recent years, the number of graduates from Yangzhou High School in Jiangsu Province who have been admitted to various famous universities in China has gradually increased, and the school's reputation has grown as a result. This year, the number of new students applying to National Central University reached 4,000, and about 600 were admitted. More than 60 graduates from the school took the entrance exam for National Central University, and as many as 54 were admitted. The results for Jiaotong University, Tsinghua University, Jinling University, and the Central Political University have not yet been announced, but it is said that a significant number of the school's applicants will also be admitted. It is reported that the school recently had 2,000 applicants, breaking all previous records. Unfortunately, there are not many places, and only about 200 students can be admitted.

Mr. Wang Yuncheng Returns Home After Completing His Studies 101

Mr. Wang Yuncheng, from Wuxi, is the son-in-law of Rong Zongjing, a magnate in the industrial sector, and the third son of Mr. Wang Yaochen, the manager of the Fuxin Flour Mill. Mr. Wang went to the United States in 1927 and entered Lowell University to specialize in textiles. He achieved outstanding results in school for several years and was praised by people in that country. He is also one of the best Chinese students studying in the United States. This summer, he obtained a Bachelor of Science degree in engineering and received an honorary award. This time, he returned home after completing his studies and will definitely use his strengths to open up new paths for the textile industry in our country. Now is the time to resist Japanese goods and promote domestic products. Textiles are especially important. Mr. Wang's return will definitely make many contributions. It is heard that Mr. Wang set off last month on the President Cleveland from the United States. After visiting factories in various places along the way, he took the President Adams back to China from Japan and is expected to arrive in Shanghai tomorrow. All of his relatives and friends here plan to go to the pier to greet him. It is also heard that various industrial groups at sea will hold a meeting to welcome him. Recent Situation of Shuren Middle School 106
