Free Talk

World Anecdotes 190

— Hai Ke

Jail Overcrowding

The new Sing Sing prison in America is the most famous prison in the world. Recently, the number of criminals has been increasing day by day, so that the number of prisoners has increased sharply and can no longer be accommodated. All short-term criminals are in the open space inside the big walls, and temporary tents are set up for them to stay temporarily. They will be released upon the expiration of their terms. All those living in prison cells are long-term prisoners.

British Widows After World War I

During the World War, the number of people who sacrificed in the participating countries was alarming. Even in the UK alone, it was not in the minority. The widows of the soldiers have no clothes or food and have to remarry. According to the investigation, in the past ten years, there have been 100,000 women who have remarried one after another. However, there are still 145,550 who have not remarried. They rely solely on the government to issue pensions to maintain their lives.

British Waiters

According to those who pay attention to social conditions, the waiters in restaurants and cafeterias all over the world, with British waiters as the first. Even the famous French waiters cannot reach them. Why is that? Because they interact with guests, they have a gentlemanly demeanor. Every move is very polite.

Nanchang Anecdotes 191

— Yang Ye Bai

The suppression of the Red Army is in full swing. Large armies are gathering in Jiangxi. Since Commander-in-Chief Chiang himself came to Gan to supervise the suppression, there are even more important party-state figures going to Gan on official business. The traffic of officials is endless. The number of civilians in the bandit areas who have fled to the province is even greater. Therefore, the new capital of Hongdu is extremely lively. I will record what I have seen and heard to tell the readers.

House Famine With the rise of the Red Army, Nanchang is full of agencies. Although the various armies have set off for the front, most of the offices and garrison offices are in the provincial capital. The families of general staff and temporary refugees are too numerous to count. Therefore, public and private houses ○ are all overcrowded. Compared with the capital, the situation is even worse.

Careful Inspection In order to strictly prevent bandits from mingling in, the authorities have been inspecting travelers with extraordinary seriousness. Car and boat docks, pay special attention. I accompanied Liu Ruiheng, a member of the National Government and chief medical supervisor of the headquarters, to Gan. When I got off the car in Nanchang, even though I presented Liu's business card and pass, it took several negotiations to avoid inspection. Its seriousness can be seen.

Anxiety Over Imaginary Problems The places where the Red Bandits entrenched themselves were burnt, killed, raped, and plundered, and it was dark. Only the order in the province was still extremely peaceful. The citizens came and went, doing nothing. Recently, the suppression of the Red Army in the front has been a great victory, and people's hearts have become more secure. A friend of mine was transferred to Gan to work a month ago. Before leaving, his wife was afraid of the communist disaster and returned to her original home in Shandong. After Mr. came to Gan, he saw that the situation was so quiet, he laughed at his wife for being too timid and good at worrying about imaginary problems.

Merchants Lucky During the suppression of the Red Army, many important and secondary figures from all sides came to Gan. There was a lot of drinking and revelry. The seats at Jiabinlou and Puyunzhai and other places were often full. The various ice drinking rooms are also ten times more profitable. In addition, Jiangxi's special products, porcelain, summer cloth, and camphor wood boxes, those who are in their place will choose to buy several things as souvenirs, or to give to relatives and friends. Therefore, the lives of general porcelain shops, summer cloth shops, woodworking shops, etc. are quite good. However, general entertainment venues such as cinemas and theaters have stopped operating due to the suppression of the Red Army. This is also fortunate and unfortunate.

The Electric Light is Blind, the Telephone is Deaf Nanchang's electric lights and telephones are not well managed. Telephones are very difficult to get through. The light of the electric lights is extremely weak. Sometimes auxiliary candles are needed. Therefore, Nanchang has the saying "the electric light is blind, the telephone is deaf". During this period of suppressing the Red Army, the work of all departments is very tense. The electric lights and telephones alone remain the same. Its conservative spirit is also worthy of many.

Maps are selling well The Red Bandits are extremely vicious, and everyone hopes that they will be eliminated as soon as possible. When the various armies are cooperating in the siege, they are extremely concerned about the military situation in the front. Everyone has a map in their hands to understand the progress situation. Generally, those who come to the province for the first time buy more Nanchang maps because they are not familiar with the roads. When I arrived in Nanchang, I asked many bookstores before I bought a map of the counties of Jiangxi. The maps of the provincial capital are all said to have been sold out long ago. The extent to which the general public cares about the situation can be seen from the sales of maps.

Lushan is affected The Lushan Mountains are a summer resort. Every summer, many Chinese and foreigners climb the mountains to escape the heat. This year, due to the suppression of the Red Army, people from all walks of life who passed through Xunyang took the time to climb the mountains. The road to Guling is twice as lively. The great mountains have suddenly increased so many uninvited guests. It is also affected by the communist disaster.

New Kidnappers Who Redeem Ransom the Same Night 192

— Huang Yingdai

Kidnapping has been prevalent in Shanghai for years. However, in recent years, such kidnapping cases have been spreading daily. Even in remote rural areas, they are heard of daily. Recently, in the area of the Mao River at the junction of Songjiang and Qingpu, kidnappers are becoming increasingly rampant, with kidnapping cases emerging one after another. The various situations are recorded below.

Kidnapping Situation: The kidnapping cases that have occurred in various villages near the Mao River this time are roughly the same. The number of people involved is about seven or eight, or more than ten. They come in a small boat in the late night or dusk. The weapons they carry are only three or four short and long guns. However, the villagers are unwise and lack the ability to resist. Moreover, even if there are kidnappers in the neighboring house, they will close their doors and not ask about it.

Definite Informants: Kidnappers must have local informants to act as accomplices, leading them into the village. Therefore, when kidnappers enter a village, they are familiar with the roads. They also know everything about the wealth and poverty of ordinary farmers. Some say that there must be a geomancer as a guide.

Ransom Redemption the Same Night: It is said that these kidnappers have no den. When kidnapping people, they can take action as soon as they seize ships along the way. After kidnapping the "God of Wealth", they wait outside the village and instruct people in the village to come to negotiate. If both parties agree on the conditions, the ransom can be redeemed that night.

Low Price: These kidnappers ask for a relatively low price. The asking price is only two or three thousand yuan, but the result is that only five or six hundred yuan is needed to settle the matter. It can be said to be a great bargain.

Place of Payment: After the kidnappers and the villagers agree on the ransom, if the villagers cannot raise a large sum of money at once, they will pay a certain amount of money that night and agree on a date to pay the remaining money. It is said that the agreed place for paying the money is mostly in the desolate tombs and chaotic graves near the Fanhua Ferry and Xujiahui stations.

Nine Out of Ten Houses Empty: Under this kind of situation, wealthy families have long been mostly empty, moving to the city. Even those who have not moved are on tenterhooks at night, sleeping in the cowshed and pigsty to avoid the attention of bandits. Even children who are only a few months old are regarded as treasures by bandits and kidnapped away. The plight of farmers is really unspeakable.

Talking About Japanese Mahjong Clubs 193

— Yisan Outer Historian

In recent years, mahjong has been extremely popular among Japanese people. Their enthusiasm is no less than that of the Americans. The Japanese authorities are afraid of creating gambling habits among the people, so they only allow it as a purely recreational game. However, those who gamble are certainly more numerous than those who do not. They often use chips as a front for winning or losing. When the game ends, money is always exchanged privately.

General speculators, catering to the psychology of the masses, are competing to establish mahjong clubs. These clubs vary in size and are spread all over the country. The names on the signs are very novel, such as "Pure One Suit", "Red Dragon", "East Wind", "Nine of Bamboo", etc. The interior decorations are extraordinarily luxurious, and there are women serving as receptionists. When the number of customers is insufficient, they can also join the game to make up the numbers. However, most of the people who go there are young men, whose intentions are not on the game itself. Moreover, the cost is not high, so the ability to attract customers is quite strong.

Some clubs, in order to promote mahjong education, hire Chinese people who are good at Japanese to serve as teachers (because mahjong was invented in China), specializing in teaching tactics for free.

A mahjong competition is held once a week. Participants must pay an entry fee of one Japanese yen per person. Then, they enter the game according to the assigned number. The first, second, and third place winners are all given valuable prizes. At the same time, the person with the worst score also receives a considerable prize. This is also a method used by the club to encourage customers who do not know how to play mahjong (no reward).

The Strange Pagoda of Wenzhou 194

— Junxia

Twenty li outside Yongjia County, there is a place called Baiyu. There is a pagoda by the river. It is about ten levels high. Its base is also very dilapidated. At a glance, one can tell that it is a building from the old century. What is strange is that the entire pagoda can automatically lean in all directions, and the direction is different every year. Therefore, the elders of the village all say that the direction the pagoda leans indicates that the people in that direction will have added happiness in that year. This kind of unfounded talk is certainly not worth discussing. However, how can a towering ancient pagoda move by itself? This is indeed strange.

Travel Notes of India (75) 195

— Linghua

In Indian religions, those who practice asceticism do not wear any clothes. Wearing clothes is not for men. Above heaven and below earth, only naked people are respected. Coming and going naked, without any attachments, is still the case today. On the banks of the Ganges, sages emerge in large numbers, still meeting each other in hundreds. Among them are not all poor and foolish people. Doctors, young masters, princes, and wealthy people abandon fame, status, and learning, even loved ones, and practice asceticism diligently. They come to the banks of the Ganges and roar to the sky to end their years. When free, they teach the masses the wonders of the Tao. Su Shi said, "The sharp edge of the Zen is not to be touched, thousands of verses are like overturning water." Those who observe the etiquette of disciples and offer incense and flowers are everywhere. This is a technique used by ancient sages to liberate themselves and the world. That is why Alexander the Great was subdued by the sages of the Jews. Alas, we can only salute and retreat. How dare we criticize it? From my point of view, two-legged animals cannot be killed no matter how hard you try, and cannot be saved no matter how hard you try. This is called society. Today, those who can kill many people are called heroes. Those who can abandon the world are also men. Are they immortals or Buddhas? Are they heroes? They are all the same monsters in the world, and they still cannot solve the problems of society.

The buildings beside the Ganges are magnificent. A certain place was built by a certain king. A certain rich man donated to it. The rooms are like combs, facing the Ganges River. The scenery is excellent. For thousands of years, sages have emerged, far surpassing the false reputation of our Zou and Lu. If we were to travel to Zou and Lu today, how many famous people could we meet? Yet the great law of the sages of the Ganges is still flourishing. Mahatma Gandhi, the new Buddha, is also a disciple of Indian religions. Alas, India's influence is like this. How dare we criticize it? In recent years, Westerners who convert to Indian religions are gradually increasing. We left the land and boarded a boat. The small boat could hold ten people. The students rowed it, letting it go into the middle of the river. We saw a red cloth package placed on the riverbank. Beside it was ash. The student said, "This package is the corpse of a dead person, which will be burned and thrown into the river to ascend to heaven." In Indian religions, heaven is in the water, while the Muslim leader Muhammad said, "Heaven is under the feet of the mother." He was speaking for the present world, while Indian religions practice asceticism and Islam follows the world. Again, an object floated in the water. The student said, "This is a corpse." I asked in surprise. He said, "This is a novice monk. After his death, people sent his body to the river, also with the intention of ascending to heaven." I wanted to vomit greatly. The Indian custom of water burial is to respect water to such an extent.

The students asked me about Chinese weddings. I said, "Now it is quite free." The student told me that in Indian customs, one can get money for marrying a wife. I asked the reason. He said, "If a person has a daughter who is not married by the age of ten, her parents will be in great trouble. If she is married, she must compensate heavily with her family property." I found it strange and asked the reason. He said, "If a daughter is not married when she is older, she will inevitably find it difficult to guard her chastity. If there is an unexpected encounter, her parents will be punished with expulsion from the clan." Aul-caste is expelled from society. If a woman has a love affair, it is considered a disgrace to the family. Therefore, people will break off relations with her family. She cannot live in society. Therefore, they are anxious to arrange early marriages, or compensate the husband's family with their family property. Men are not in a hurry to marry early. Therefore, families with daughters are very worried. In Indian customs, one never divorces in one's life. Widows often commit suicide after their husbands die, considering it common. I find the Indian ideal strange. In everything, they create a fixed system of fate, nailing all living people to a fixed law within the system, and maintaining it to this day. The best remedy for this kind of system is Western free marriage and love to counteract it. How strange it is. The student said, "Now, influenced by the Western wind, it is gradually changing."

There was a student who did not believe in any gods. I said, "Look at the temples by the river, many have fallen. The gods cannot even protect their own temples. They must rely on people to protect the gods."

Rotary Club of Fiction

Women Women (10) 196

— Yao Sufeng

"Well, you keep watch! Mr. Lu, who came yesterday, will probably come again today!" Miss Ding said softly. Qiu Zi also smiled and agreed.

Before long, Mr. Lu indeed arrived. Qiu Zi saw him from a distance as she stood at the gate and immediately went inside to inform. When Mr. Lu walked into the reception room, Miss Ding was already smiling as she greeted him.

"I'm too late! I hope you don't mind," Mr. Lu's gentle tone and courteous manner strongly stimulated Miss Ding's fragile emotions.

"I've been waiting for a long time! I thought you might have had something else to do," said Miss Ding.

"Could anything be more important than coming here today, in all that I do? Before I came, I was so worried and timid...I just thought, maybe I would end up disappointing you. But now, I have boldly come, and boldly brought something with me. Will you despise me? Or will you pity me?" Mr. Lu had indeed put a lot of thought into these words, which were very tactful and natural, like the song of a begging little bird.

At the same time, a small diamond ring in his pocket appeared before Miss Ding's eyes. Miss Ding showed no other expression than a smile. She said, "What does this mean?"

"This is my contribution. I hope it can be exchanged for the most precious thing in the world, which is your love," said Mr. Lu, with every word trembling like a wave.

Miss Ding could not help but show shyness. But in her unspoken silence, it was clear that she had accepted Mr. Lu's request. Mr. Lu gently took her hand and gently stroked it. She seemed to want to avoid it, but seemed to let Mr. Lu do as he pleased.

Five minutes later, Miss Ding's left middle finger was already wearing the diamond ring that Mr. Lu had brought. They looked at each other, their eyes seemingly flowing with water and burning with fire.

Qiu Zi waited outside the door. She clearly knew that there was a mysterious meaning in the reception room, but she did not dare to rush in rashly. She secretly peeked through the keyhole. She saw Mr. Lu and her young lady sitting side by side. She also saw Mr. Lu put a ring on her young lady's hand. She also saw Mr. Lu lower his head and kiss her young lady's hand… Her heart could not help but beat wildly.

Finally, she heard them calling her from the room. She walked in and saw that her young lady's face was covered with a blush of shyness, which she could not hide, even though she was being very reserved.

Finance 197

Gold Standard Continues to Show Weakness 198

Slight Decline: Yesterday, the Gold Industry Exchange opened as usual. The gold standard declined slightly, and the situation was still stable, hovering around 40 taels. The overall market had a turnover of 5 taels, eventually falling by 2.1 taels. The silver market rose slightly in the morning, but market sentiment was weak, and the market opened low, soon breaking through 40 taels. Afterwards, the exchange rate loosened and then stabilized. On the surface, the buying side seemed to be active. By noon, the 40-tael mark was regained. There were slight advances and retreats, and the afternoon market was more peaceful, but the fluctuations were very small, and trading was scattered. There may be no glory or disgrace for the major firms this morning.

Morning Opens Low: The opening price for September this morning fell by 4.3 mace, to 737.5 taels. There were no changes in the major firms and silver prices from the 2nd. On the 3rd, London was closed, but the New York silver price rose by 1/8, with a private telegram adding 1/16. In addition, Citibank's stock was reported to be high, so the intention of the industry was further downward. Zhifengyong, Qianchangxiang, Wupin, etc. all sold, eventually falling to 36.5 taels. Not long after, Dalian Bank and Cuichangyong, Yuancheng, etc. bought in, and Zhengjin initially absorbed 1,875 taels of October British gold. Later, Maihang and Zhejiang traded August 125. Therefore, the gold price rose slowly, a total increase of 4 mace, to 40.04 taels at 9:20 AM. The British gold price was announced unchanged. During the period, Wupin hedged and sold, falling to 39 taels. Afterwards, Yuanheng, Yuanchengyong, and Cuichangyong came in, and China Bank absorbed 125 of October British gold, and Mitsui absorbed 1.61 to 1.60875 taels of Japanese gold, so the price rose by about 2 mace again, reaching 39.9 mace at 9:30 AM. A moment later, Yuanmaoyong and others sold, and Taiwan bought 1.6075 taels of Japanese gold, and a forward price of 1.6125 taels appeared again, falling by 1 mace. At 10:30 AM, the price was 38.7 mace. The situation tended to stabilize afterwards. Cuichangyong, Yongfeng, Changshengyong, speculator Wu, etc. all bought in, so the price seemed to rise. Soon after, the Indian exchange rate fell by 2 annas, making it even more firm. At 11:30 AM, the price was 40.08 taels, but Shunli, Wanxing, and Yuanmaoyong sold out. At the close of the market, the price was 40 taels, and the quoted price was still 790.02 taels, a difference of about 50 taels.

Falls 2.1 Taels: The after-market opened at 40.05 taels, but Wupin had already opened at 0.05 taels, then rose from 0.07 taels to 0.02 taels. It was then heard that the Indian exchange rate was down by 1 anna, and Cuichangyong, Dadecheng, etc. bought in, jumping by more than 1 tael, reaching 41.5 taels at 2:20 PM. After that, HSBC sold 125 of British gold, and Zhifengyong, Fuchang, etc. sold out, immediately falling by 1 tael, reaching 40.02 taels after 2:30 PM, and 0.089 taels after 3:00 PM. Afterwards, there were very few transactions, and the exchange rate did not change. The British gold price of 125 could be settled. Yuanmaoyong, Tongfengheng, etc. sold out, immediately falling back to within 40 taels, reaching 39.2 taels after 4:00 PM, then rising by 6-7 mace, to 39.9 taels. At the close of the market at 4:30 PM, the price was 39.7 taels, a decrease of 2.1 taels compared to last Saturday (August 1). The maximum price during the day was 41.5 taels, and the minimum price was 36.5 taels, a difference of 5 taels.

Spot Market Still Stable: The early market price for Wupin was 37.3 taels, 40.05 taels in the afternoon, 0.05 taels in the afternoon, and the closing price was 39.8 taels. As for the money industry, although there were daily inflows and outflows, the bank closures were naturally slightly more than usual. However, the market price of foreign cash turned higher in the early market and was still weak in the afternoon market. The silver dismantling also occupied a dominant position. The situation on the auxiliary currency was still not much different.

Securities: Government Bonds Rebound 203

Decline of Around Half a Yuan

Yesterday, the government bond market on the local stock exchange saw limited trading in spot bonds, with only the demobilization of soldiers bond showing some activity. The futures market remained buoyant. Trading volume in the morning was lively, reaching 15.6 million between the two sessions. In the afternoon, the market was calmer with less price volatility. Bond prices experienced a slight correction, and fluctuations were more moderate. With bond prices having already risen significantly, some market participants took profits by selling at the high. Additionally, certain parties continued to offload positions, resulting in a general decline at the opening. Long-term unified tax bonds had once fallen by more than one yuan, but the supply and demand dynamics normalized, and prices stabilized. Fluctuations in each session were minimal, with only customs bonds showing some firmness and most others falling by about 0.45 yuan. The price movements seemed to have reached a temporary pause. Total spot bond trading volume for the day was only 8,000 yuan, while futures trading reached 23.4 million yuan, with the unified tax bond being the most active and the 20-year customs bond also accounting for a significant portion.

Yarn Market Shows Slight Improvement 204

The yarn market is slightly firmer, and the trend is still stable. This is because the overseas cotton yarn situation is temporarily leaning towards the downstream, causing a lack of confidence. However, buyers see that foreign cotton has fallen for several days in a row, and anticipate a possible rebound. Furthermore, two yarn factories in Wuxi have stopped for repairs and reorganization, and there are rumors of a strike. As a result, the market sentiment has slightly improved. However, current yarn sales are unusually sluggish, and all businesses have been affected by floods, showing no signs of excitement. In addition, the floods in various provinces are becoming more severe, severely impacting autumn sales. Nevertheless, judging from the overall situation, it is difficult for prices to rise significantly.

Individual Investors Make Purchases: In the forward market of the Exchange, the opening situation was flat, but later individual investors made purchases, and prices for various months rose slightly by two, three, four, and five cents. The afternoon market sentiment was still stable, and prices for various months rose another four cents. The total transaction volume was 20,900 bales. According to reports, Xincheng sold 1,050 bales, Minghua 800 bales, Jifeng 500 bales, Mingde 550 bales, and Lichang 550 bales. Mingde bought 1,000 bales, Yiyu 1,200 bales, and Gengfeng 1,100 bales. The closing prices of the forward market are recorded on the left.

Cotton Market Shows Slight Improvement 205

The American cotton situation is still flat, but local sentiment is slightly firmer. This is because American cotton has fallen for eight consecutive days, and there is concern that it may rebound and rise. In addition, there is news that 1.3 million bales of American cotton have been loaned to Germany, and there is concern that this may become a reality. Individual investors are therefore competing to buy, and the market trend is becoming slightly tighter. However, judging from the overall situation, it is still normal. This is because the spot price of American cotton, calculated in silver, is only about 35.8 taels, so large players are unanimously selling. However, due to floods in various regions, cotton losses are not small. How the future will unfold depends on exchange rate fluctuations and the performance of American cotton.

Rice Market in Hexia Falls Sharply Again 208

South Market: Yesterday, the sources from various businesses totaled about twenty, mostly from Pinghu and Nangang, with a small amount from Pudong. Retail sales in urban and rural areas were sluggish. The arrival of Dongxin japonica rice saw a surge in supply, and sentiment was flat, reducing the intention to buy. Businesses also felt more relaxed due to the fatigue in the North Market, and transactions were limited. Selling prices had to be lowered, with thick indica and thin japonica prices falling by two to three corners. There was not much of the top-grade yanglu pointed rice, and sales were also thin. However, as the amount of foreign rice increased again, the market was firm. Yin rice was uplifted by the Tongbian Company, and fresh high-quality rice continued to be sold, with market prices being strong. 170-180 shih of Pudong new japonica rice arrived yesterday. As for retail sales, they were extremely weak, and prices fell by another half a yuan. The reason for the high price of foreign rice is that supplies have been scarce for a long time, and there is little stock in warehouses. The actions of out-of-town businesses are not sufficient to meet demand, and the market situation has stabilized.

Xinzha: The rice market had more than thirty sources, but sales were in a slump. The new japonica rice market has been weakening daily, with ordinary goods down half a yuan. The situation still requires further declines. Early indica rice is arriving in abundance but sales are sluggish, falling back by three to four corners. Sales of thick japonica rice are becoming increasingly rare, and warehouse stocks are gradually increasing. Buying interest is muted. Top-grade Yanglu pointed rice is arriving continuously, with some inquiries for small lots. Production reports continue to soften. The above prices have all fallen by one to two corners, and the market situation is extremely weak. The price of top-grade rice at the port is slightly lower, so businesses still have a strong appetite. The situation is slightly soft, and a small amount of top-grade rice is sold by out-of-towners, with few transactions. However, the sources seem to be becoming scarcer, and the shortage of white yuan goods is increasing daily by two to three chi.

Flour Market Rises and Then Softens 209

Yesterday, the flour market initially showed a firm trend but then weakened. This is because the quoted price of foreign wheat fell slightly by one to two corners, and there are very large stocks of American wheat, with a tendency to dump them. Therefore, although the buying interest from inland businesses was very strong at the opening, mostly due to the floods, concentrating their strength, factories had foreign wheat contracted and gradually unloaded it, so the market rose and then softened. As a result, the price for August was 2.5 li better than the previous day, the price for September was 7.5 li better, and the prices for October to January were 2.5 li better, it is said.

Wheat Market Temporarily Presents a Stalemate 210

Yesterday, the wheat futures market generally showed a hovering trend. The quoted price of foreign wheat fell again slightly by one to two corners. Although inland businesses were still firm in their intentions due to the continued floods, the shorts had foreign wheat available to deliver, so both sides had strength in the stalemate. As a result, transactions became quiet and the market saw little up or down movement. In the end, only the price for October was up slightly by two fen, the price for November was up slightly by one fen, and there were no changes for the rest. Because factory demand is still good, the price of spot wheat is trending stable. Over five thousand bags of wheat from Wusong, Shuangfeng, Taicang, Zhitang, Huangdu, Anting, Penglai, Nanjing, Zhenjiang, and Jiangyan were purchased by Fuxin and Huafeng, it is said.

Silk and Tea: Shanghai Factory Transactions Were Scarce in July 211

Only a total of 140 bales were transacted... Sales to British, French, and Silk Businesses

The Shanghai white factory products handled by foreign firms in this port and sales to America have been stagnant for several months. Britain and France also only had sporadic spot transactions. The appetite of inland silk businesses was even smaller. Transactions in July were scarce, with only 140 bales of spot silk transacted. Sales to Britain and France accounted for 80% of the total, with the remainder purchased by silk merchants from Zhejiang and Hangzhou, it is said.

European and American Silk Sales Are Almost Stagnant 212

The cable from European and American Hua silk yesterday still showed no signs of turning around. The European firms in the Shanghai port did not dare to take risks and proceed. Yesterday, only inland silk merchants purchased 5 bales of Shanghai white factory spot products and 5 bales of lower-grade dried silk, and prices were firm, it is said.

Green Tea Market Trend is Increasingly Firm 213

Yesterday, in the tea market in this port, European firms continued to have a strong need for green tea such as Zhenmei and Zhenmei needles from Lailu. The price of core-drawn Zhenmei has been raised to 230 taels, and the market trend is increasingly firm. Shrimp eyes, Fengmei, etc., also have good sales, and the market price has been raised by four to five taels. Regarding Gongxi, the Russian Aid Society is said to continue reviewing it today and begin negotiating prices. According to the general intention of tea merchants, this year's harvest in the interior has been greatly reduced, and they are unwilling to compromise and sell the tea, it is said.

Piece Goods: Chinese Factory Cotton Cloth Prices Rise Sharply 214

Local Factory Cloth: The recent trend has been very chaotic. The goods from Chinese factories have a tendency to soar to the sky due to the impact of the boycott of Japanese goods, especially fine cloth and fine twill, which are even more scarce and expensive. Compared to before the boycott, they must rise by six or seven cents. Yesterday, Balloon fine cloth sold for 7 taels and 9.5 mace, Ren Zhong for 7 taels and 8.5 mace, Jincheng fine twill for 8 taels and 1.5 mace, and Butterfly Ball for 7 taels and 7.5 mace. Furthermore, spot goods are extremely scarce. Since the smooth sales of Japanese factory goods before the boycott, spot goods have also been extremely scarce, so they have not fallen recently. After once rising, coarse cloth has gradually stabilized. 9-pound Five Blessings is 5 taels and 1.5 mace, 11-pound Ren Zhong is 5 taels and 7 mace, 13-pound Double Horse is 6 taels and 6.5 mace, and 16-pound Five Cranes is 8 taels and 2.5 mace, it is said.

East and West Piece Goods: Although Eastern goods have been under severe boycott for the past few days, sales are still smooth. The Yangtze River basin is even busier than usual. This is because although Shanghai has implemented inspections, the ports of Hankou, Shashi, Changsha, and Chongqing are still unimpeded, so the firms in Shanghai are entrusting Japanese customs brokers to pack and transport goods, so prices have not fallen. However, as of yesterday, the Hankou businesses have sent a telegram to stop packing and handling goods due to the floods. A large batch of goods was sent to Sichuan and Changsha yesterday, and a batch of transit goods has recently been handled for the businesses in Yunnan and Guizhou. The equivalent Western goods are very scarce in the market, so development is difficult to predict, it is said.

North and South Goods: Quanzhou Pao Yuan (Dried Longan) Prices Rise 215

Quanzhou pao yuan has been in short supply recently. The stock of the firms has already been baked, increasing costs. Now that the local stock is scarce and the new crop is still far away, businesses are quite interested in buying. Several hundred boxes of top-grade round longan have been transacted daily, with prices rising by two to three taels compared to before. However, the firms' stock is already scarce, so the market is expected to rise rather than fall, it is said.

Automobile News

Commentary

General Discussion of the Feixia Car 238

--- Dumb

The current development situation of various automobile factories in Italy is rapidly advancing. Among them, the progress of the Feixia factory is particularly astonishing. If we recall ten years ago, the Feixia factory was not well-known at that time, and the performance of the cars produced was also very ordinary. However, in the recent ten years, there has been special progress. The cars produced over the years have all been well-received by society. Sales have increased year by year. Nowadays, almost every city center has Feixia cars. In short, Feixia cars are truly unique in the automobile market, especially among small cars, and have already established a significant position. Since the end of the European War, Feixia has launched the 501 model. Because of its excellent performance, it has been widely welcomed by society. Following the 501, there were also the 509, 514, and 521 models. The new cars launched each year have shown remarkable progress, which is why sales have been so prosperous.

Looking at the past history of Feixia cars, the beauty of the design and the spaciousness of the interior are probably the most obvious features of the various new models. Almost everyone knows this. Among them, the 514 model stands out with its unprecedented beautiful body. Although the wheelbase is no different from the nine-horsepower Feixia car, the interior space of the car is slightly wider. Even with four people sitting inside, it feels very comfortable, with no feeling of crowding. The aluminum radiator, tall and narrow, also enhances the vehicle's aesthetic appeal. The body's construction is particularly surprising. The four-door sedan has three lights on each side. The two-door coupe has two large windows. Other models, such as convertibles and two-seater sedans, all have very comfortable seats, and the exterior of the body is painted in a very elegant and beautiful manner. In short, the beautiful appearance and comfortable driving of Feixia cars are unmatched by any other car.

In addition, the main advantages of Feixia's latest cars lie in the exquisite engine and powerful electrical system. The electrical system, governed by the generator, battery, and coil, distributes current very conveniently and also has a relatively strong generating power. As for the engine construction, it is particularly unique. There are four main points in the way the chassis is connected, with spherical rubber devices in between to act as cushioning. The distribution method places two of these points near the meshing gear, which are the key connection points. The other two points are in the front and extend over the car frame. The simple meshing gear is fitted with an elliptical handle, which operates very smoothly and requires no attention. The gearbox is made of lead and has four acceleration settings. Moreover, the place where it connects with the meshing gear is also connected with screws, as are various other important parts. In addition, the small gears, covered with a mesh, ensure that there is no noise when the car is running. There are truly countless advantages.

Following the 514 model, Feixia soon launched a six-wheeled, six-cylinder bus. Its excellent performance was unprecedented. It was once displayed at the Italian branch of the Milan factory for public exhibition. In terms of Italy's current transportation industry, it is no different from other European countries. In bustling cities, buses are used for transportation instead of streetcars. This is especially true in Rome, the capital of Italy. Currently, in busy areas of Rome, only buses are allowed, and streetcars are prohibited. Other central areas, such as Milan, Florence, and Naples, have also adopted the same policy, although not as strictly as Rome. It can be seen that the sales of buses in Italy are undoubtedly considerable. The new Feixia large-wheel bus is the 604 model, manufactured in Italy. Since

Discussion of the Carriage Decoration of Sedan Automobiles 239

— Yu Xiang

The increasing sophistication of modern life into artistry is an undeniable fact. All objects are valued for their beautiful decoration, to move people. Westerners often like to come up with unique ideas for their daily automobiles, adding some decoration as a point of pride. In particular, the interiors of sedan automobiles feature many novel and exquisite adornments, greatly enhancing the refined taste. Here, a few examples are specially selected for car owners in Shanghai to draw inspiration from.

Fragrance Filling the Seats: The extravagance of French women's lives has long been known. Their fondness for perfume is particularly intense. Not only is their jade-like skin constantly fragrant, but their clothes and residences are also often sprinkled with perfume to attract the opposite sex. Not long ago, in Paris, whenever women drove by in their cars, a strong scent of perfume would spread through the air, intoxicating and captivating. This is because they also liberally sprinkle perfume in the car, resulting in the seats being filled with fragrance and the allure overflowing. As for women in the British Isles, they are inherently quiet and fond of nature, and do not like strong perfumes. Therefore, they often keep one or two fresh flowers in their cars. The delicate fragrance slowly wafts, with an elegance beyond compare, creating a completely different atmosphere from the French women in Paris.

A Dazzling Array of Portraits: Photographs and portraits, in modern life, are a form of decoration with considerable authority. The practice of hanging portraits inside automobile carriages originated in America. Now, it is commonly seen in continental Europe. These portraits are mostly very exquisite and delicate, occupying very little space inside the car, yet they are dazzling and extremely lovely. The people in the portraits generally have a very close relationship with the car owner, hence they cannot bear to be separated for even a moment. American young men and women, in particular, often hang pictures of their loved ones inside the car to dispel loneliness. Last autumn, in Chicago, a major tragedy unfortunately occurred as a result of this. An American girl named Carlson, while driving, constantly gazed at the photograph of her smiling lover hanging inside the car. She was momentarily negligent and injured a pedestrian, ultimately receiving a prison sentence of several months before being released.

Brocade Curtains and Cushions: The exquisite and ingenious silk embroidery of the Orient has long been treasured by Europeans and Americans. In recent years, the export of embroidery from our country to overseas markets, sold in Europe and America, has increased significantly each year. According to surveys, the largest buyers of this category of embroidery are the Americans, followed by various countries in continental Europe. Those used as curtains and cushions inside sedan automobiles account for as much as six or seven tenths. The popularity of this trend at the time can be imagined.

Recent Conditions of Guizhou Province's Roads 240

— Shanlang

The Construction Department of Guizhou Province, recognizing that the stagnation of customs, the poverty of the people, and the depletion of wealth are due to inconvenient transportation, has recently been actively working to develop the roads. Now, I explore and record news of various roads below.

(1) Sandu Road: Sandu Road starts from Duyun County, passes through the territories of Maha and Bazhai Counties, and ends at Sanhe, for a total length of over one hundred eighty li. Sanhe has a navigable river that leads directly to Liuzhou and Wuzhou in Guangxi, connecting with the main confluence of the Pearl River, which is also the main transportation route between Guizhou and Guangxi. Currently, the project is actively underway in four sections. I will describe the general situation below. (1) Duyun Section: The entire section is about seventy li long. The roadbed work has been fully connected. Although there are some places that need minor corrections, they are not very difficult. There are no major special projects. Therefore, not much funding is needed, and the work is convenient. It can be completed in a short period. The section from Pulin Street to Yagong Pass is already passable, and the rock excavation project at Yagong Pass has also been completed. (2) Maha

Page 20

Section: The entire section is about twenty li long. The roadbed work has not yet begun. The largest bridges, such as the one over Wengcheng River, require the construction of ten stone bridges. Yu Sihe River is about sixty zhang wide and is the largest project on this branch road. This section is the largest project and requires the most funding. Without guaranteed funding, it is difficult to determine a completion date. (3) Bazhai Section: The entire section is about thirty li long. Nearly six thousand five hundred laborers are currently engaged in surfacing with gravel, deepening side ditches, and tidying up roadside stones. The entire section is about seven tenths completed. However, the Taiyuan Bridge is damaged and still needs to be repaired, and the Taiyuan Slope also needs rock excavation. Once these two places are repaired, it can be passable. (4) Sanhe Section: The entire section is about fifty li long. The roadbed and surface are about eight tenths completed. What needs to be repaired now is the rock excavation at Yangyong Pass and the embankment construction at Daoma Kan. Once these two places are completed, it can also be passable.

(2) Luxia Road: Luxia Road is about sixty li long. It starts from Lujia Bridge in Maha County, passes through the territory of Lushan County, and connects to Xiasi. Xiasi also has a navigable river that flows through Hunan into Hankou, which is an important transportation route between Guizhou and Hunan. Here is a brief description of the construction progress. The section belonging to Maha County is about forty li long. The roadbed has been connected, and the surface is also being prepared. The project is simple and can be completed in a short period. The section belonging to Lushan County is only a little over ten li long, but the Huaqiao Bridge project is larger and requires more funding. Fortunately, the roadbed has been connected. Once the bridge work is completed, the entire road can be passable. As for the branch road section from Xiasi to Sifangjing, earth and stone work is currently underway in three groups. The first group is building a five-chi-high and seven-zhang-long road embankment on the left side of the Xiasi Market entrance, which has already been completed. The second group is excavating three cubic zhang of rocks at the Guanyinge entrance, of which one cubic zhang has been completed. The third group is digging the high slope on the right side of the Yandong Slope and filling the low-lying areas on the left side, which has been completed for ten zhang.

(3) Guiyang, Guiding Phoenix Mountain Area: In the Phoenix Mountain area of Guiding, there are currently over a hundred laborers working on the extremely steep slopes of the mountain and the nearby side ditches, and carrying stone materials and digging mud at the Tuidi Datong and Yakou areas. The laborers are quite enthusiastic. There are also over twenty stonemasons excavating over four hundred cubic chi of rocks. Both sides of Guanyintang have arched over one zhang. The Guiding Xima River Bridge has been completed for one span and the Shamujian span. The remaining three spans can be completed within one or two weeks. The Tangjiazai Bridge has been completed for one span, and the remaining two spans are half completed. The rocks at Guanyinge are excavated to an average length of ten zhang and a depth of three chi. From Guiding Wengcheng Bridge to Shimenkan, there were over nine hundred laborers and two hundred and fifty stonemasons this week. The laborers are digging at the Shimenkan entrance and the concave entrance of Phoenix Mountain and carrying mud and waste rocks. The stonemasons are excavating about one thousand cubic chi of rocks at the Datong Yakou. The Guanyin Bridge has been fully sharpened.

(4) Gui'an Road: Gui'an Road, the Guiyang section from Qige Majiaoyin to Shihuiyao, has many road rocks. Team Leader Zhang of the road engineering team has surveyed and disclosed the results as follows. (1) Above Qige Majiaoyin, side ditch rocks should be excavated, totaling eighty-four zhang in length, three chi in width, and two chi in depth. (2) The slope of Xin Street should be reduced, and road rocks and side ditches on both sides should be excavated, totaling twenty-four zhang in length, three zhang six chi in width (including side ditches on both sides of the road), and three chi in depth. (3) The slope of Mawang Temple should be excavated, totaling fourteen zhang in length, three zhang six chi in width, and six chi three cun in depth. (4) The side ditch below Mawang Temple should have rock excavation, totaling nine zhang in length and three chi in width. (5) The right side ditch of Baihua Mountain should have rock excavation, totaling four zhang five chi in length, three chi in width, and four chi in height. (6) The left side ditch of Baihua Mountain should have rock excavation, totaling nine zhang in length, three chi in width, and two chi in depth. (7) The slope of Shihuiyao should have rock excavation, totaling eighteen zhang in length, three chi six cun in width, and five chi in depth. (8) The left side ditch of Shihuiyao should have rock excavation, totaling eighteen zhang in length, three chi in width, and two chi in depth. The road is currently undergoing active work. The section below Qige Majiaoyin, about thirty zhang, has been fully completed. The road surface completed in the Gan Tian area of Erpu is about four hundred and eighty zhang. The section from Shihuiyao to Huiyuan Bridge has been paved with eighty zhang of gravel. Seventy zhang have been paved at the two places of Paifangbian and Guansheng Temple. Eighty zhang have been paved at the two places of Guigui Tuo and Yeyatang. Ninety zhang have been paved from Yangliushu to Chayuan. The completed area from Datie Street to Sanpu is about seventy zhang. The completed area from Shatian to Shiguan is about two hundred and fifty zhang. The rock excavation for the newly built stone scholar at Haozhitang is about one hundred and fifty zhang. (5) Guinan Road: Zhou Bingji, the Guinan Road project director, recently submitted a letter to the construction department's road office, stating that except for a few special projects in the Machangping to Huoshan area, work is being actively expedited. The road should be passable in early May. In addition to the previous report, the road conditions from Machangping to Guiyang are described below for review. First, within the territory of Pingyue, the Xiahe Bridge has arched six sets of rocks. Due to the handover of the old and new county magistrates, the laborers suddenly dispersed, causing a slight pause. Now, the newly appointed Mr. Chen has strictly ordered the matter to be handled. Both civil and stone work are progressing simultaneously and can be completed in early May. One span of Sanwan Bridge has been sealed. The other span is only four sets of rocks away from being sharpened and can be completed by the end of this month. As for the road surface and other obstacles, they have long been cleared and repaired separately. However, there are still quite a few places with excessively steep slopes and major projects. Due to environmental and economic reasons, it is currently impossible to thoroughly clear and repair them. If only seeking to make the road passable, it can be done in early May. Second, within the territory of Guiding, the Mouqiudong Bridge was completed long ago. The five-span bridge outside the West Gate is currently under construction. Upon returning to Guiding, the responsible authorities have ordered the district to ensure that the wooden frame is complete and that the stones are transported. As for the stonemasons, in addition to strictly ordering the Lan stonemason leader to actively proceed, they have also ordered two other stonemason leaders, Luo and He, who are working on other bridges, to separate out two spans. With the increase in stonemasons, the laborers can seriously assist, so the road can also be passable in early May. The first two or three bridges have long been completed. In summary, the Guiding project, except for the slight obstacle of the five-span bridge, the remaining routes can be forcibly passable. However, due to environmental and economic reasons, the slopes are too steep, and the projects are too large, such as the Gu Meng Pass, Guanyin Pavilion, Shimenkan, and Zaojiao Ya areas, which are really beyond what can be thoroughly done at present. Third, within the territory of Longli, the bridges have long been completed. The road rock project is also over half completed. It is no longer a question that it will be passable soon. Fourth, within the territory of Guiyang, please supervise it nearby, and it can be passable in early May. I will return to Pingyue today to urge the project to proceed.

Youth Garden

Tiger 241

— Wen Qing

In countries below the equator, everywhere is dense forest, and even in villages, towns or plains, the deep green shadows closely obscure everything. If you climb up the mountains and hills, you can hardly see the sun.

The industrial town of Sushima is surrounded by mountains on three sides and faces the sea on one side. There are many tigers and monkeys on the mountains. When the sky is overcast, their mournful cries and long howls in the mountains are very poignant, but the scholars or overseas Chinese who hear these sounds do not take them seriously, just like shepherds hearing the bleating of mountain goats. When I first arrived there, I found these sounds very strange and frightening. I used to love to wander by the coconut trees, and I also liked to sit under the wisteria flowers. As a result, I was a little afraid to go out.

The school is located on the mountainside, surrounded by old trees that are hundreds of years old. The mountain road newly built by the Dutch government not only makes it convenient for pedestrians and vehicles to travel, but also provides many conveniences for tigers. Every night, when it is quiet, they run from the mountains to the road to take a walk, look at the electric lights hanging on both sides, and listen to the scholars' music. They don't cry or make noise, as if they are afraid of waking people's sweet dreams. One day at dusk, the tigers and monkeys cried particularly sadly, so I asked a newly acquainted friend,

"Miss Zhang, the tigers and monkeys are crying particularly fiercely today. I don't know what the reason is."

"Because they feel too lonely living in the deep mountains for a long time, and they want to come down and see the electric lights, but they don't have money."

"If I were the general manager of a movie theater, maybe I would invite them into the theater."

"Miss Liu is really generous."

I asked her a serious question, which led her to make a joke with me. Indeed, I am really afraid of tigers. A few months ago, in a zoo in Java, I saw three tigers the size of small yellow cattle, confined in a large iron cage. When they saw the tourists, they turned their backs viciously like mules. Each of the patterned hairs stood on their backs like small trees. They also opened their blood basins like mouths, revealing silver teeth half a foot long, and made violent shouts at us. They also raised their two front paws high and placed them on the thick iron bars, while leaning their big heads against the gaps in the iron bars, drilling outwards in a frenzy. If they could run out, I am afraid that each tiger would not be full even after eating ten people. Because that time the tigers gave me a very deep impression, I am particularly afraid of tigers.

After some time, my friend Huiqing came. I told her about the news of many tigers in the mountains, and she couldn't help but feel afraid, almost not daring to go out the door. Our dormitory is isolated, a small, low house, deeply buried under the coconut trees. Because the weather is very hot, I only close the windows and doors at nine o'clock every night. Huiqing is afraid that tigers will run into the room to forage for food, so whenever the setting sun falls behind the volcano and the shadows chase away the dusk, she closes the windows and doors tightly.

There is no air circulation in the house, and it is extremely hot. With a fan in my hand, I can't do anything. Therefore, I feel very annoyed in my heart. I said bluntly,

"Before you came, I lived here alone, and the tigers didn't eat me. Do you want to be the queen?"

"A skinny bone like you, the tigers are afraid of breaking their teeth."

"You don't seem to be very fat. Look in the mirror and you will know that tigers must love to eat your meat. Unless they notify you in advance, like the school's maid, who weighs one hundred and sixty-two pounds, she still runs back and forth on the road at night, and she hasn't run into the tiger's mouth yet."

"Don't talk nonsense to me. I am really annoyed. I originally decided to return home via Bataan, but you sent letter after letter, urging my soul, and urging me to this tiger's den, suffering all the horror. I want to go back, I will leave tomorrow, lest I be buried in the belly of a tiger."

"Okay, don't make a fuss. If the tigers hear it, they will run over to find food for supper. It's already eleven o'clock, and our bodies and minds seem to be very tired. We have to get up at seven o'clock tomorrow to go to class. Let's go to sleep."

I said a few words, and she seemed to be very considerate of my fatigue. She didn't say a word, silently paced around the house a few times, and then fell asleep on the bed.

At school, there are six full hours of homework every day, starting at seven o'clock in the morning and continuing until one o'clock in the afternoon. Only on Saturdays are there only five hours. In the last hour, the student union holds a speech competition. Usually, I can rest for an hour, but on the Saturday of the twelfth week, it was my turn to judge. After the students finished their speeches, I also pretended to be a teacher and climbed onto the stage to criticize their language, tone, meaning, and attitude. There were more than two hundred students in the whole hall, all gathered attentively in a large auditorium. Unexpectedly, on the left side of the school's playground, a tiger came from somewhere, with its tail between its legs, sitting under a big elephant tree, its head facing the glass window, as if someone had invited it to listen to the speech. This was seen by a male student who went out to urinate. When he ran in, jumping and shouting, the air in the hall was almost completely destroyed. When everyone ran out to see, the tiger's body had already received three bullets from the bayonet of a Dutchman. It stretched out its four legs and fell under the tree, breathing its last breath.

Although there are many tigers in this mountain, I have never seen such a strange thing. After this incident, it also caused people in the whole village to discuss it. Some said it was a divine tiger, and some said it was a ghost tiger. These are all unfounded judgments. Some people say that tigers are afraid of earthquakes, because there was an earthquake a week ago, so the tiger was a little scared and ran down the mountain to escape, unfortunately escaping to the bayonet of a Dutchman.

At that time, Huiqing became even more frightened. Not only did she have to close the doors tightly at night, but she also dared not go out the door during the day. When she saw the mass of fresh blood flowing from the tiger's wound on the lawn under the elephant tree, she couldn't help but feel terrified.

When the weather is hot and irritable, you have to eat more ice water and fruits. Every time I want to go down the mountain to buy fruits, she always forbids me to go. Sometimes when I insisted on going down the mountain, she always cursed like this,

"If you are not buried under the volcano, you will be buried in the tiger's mouth. I don't care, go ahead."

"No, don't worry too much."

"This doesn't seem to have anything to do with me, but if you don't return home with me during the summer vacation, then I should also write a letter to your mother, telling her in detail about the news of your illness here and the current environment, because when we came out, your mother treated me like your older sister, entrusting me to take care of you, because you are too childish."

"Please don't let her know about these things. I will go with you during the summer vacation."

"Well, that's good."

At that time, I promised to return home with her, and she immediately opened her eyebrows and a smile hung on her lips. If I hadn't been ill and had travel expenses before, I might have returned home long ago, because there, in addition to the two dangers of tigers and volcanoes, there are many intangible oppressions, like the oppression that a timid nation should endure. From that day on, I had firmly decided that in two months, I would no longer want to hear the mournful sounds of tigers roaring and monkeys crying in the deep mountains.

Youth Garden Submission Guidelines 242

(1) The text should focus on discussions of youth issues, news about domestic and foreign schools or students, essays, descriptions of school life, and pen dignity as the scope, and the style is not limited.

(2) Books are limited to those on youth issues.

(3) Photos that qualify are youth life (such as sports travel, swimming, gatherings, exhibitions, various competitions, etc.), school news, and youth sports, regardless of individual groups, are welcome. Do not write on both sides of the manuscript paper.

(4) The number of words in each article should not exceed two thousand.

(5) The manuscript should be written horizontally, not in a sloppy manner. Western words should be omitted if possible. If it is necessary to cite the original text, it must be attached below the translation.

The Chinese Cotton Textile Factory announced that the raw materials for raising hair, such as thistle fruits, used by the factory have been imported from Japan. The profits and rights have been flowing overseas, and the numbers are actually quite large. He specially purchased seeds and returned to China, vigorously urging farmers to cultivate the seeds. Over the years, the results have been excellent, and the thistle fruits are even more durable than Japanese goods. The price is also very cheap, and it has been repeatedly praised by Chinese cotton textile factories. Now, in order to promote domestic products, 100,000 units have been loaded and sent to Shanghai to meet the needs of cotton textile factories. If you want to purchase, contact No. 43, Chungeng Lane, Xiqipan Street, this city.

The society, in view of the fact that there is a lack of high-quality inks among domestic products, so that patriots have no way to buy them, and the profits and rights flow overseas, does not know how many.
